Ruling on the Jinan Telephone Company Lawsuit 83

Court Rejects Japanese Application

Jinan Dispatch: In the case of debt disputes between the Japanese East Asia Development Company and the Jinan Telephone Company, the Jinan District Court previously ordered the Telephone Company to repay the Japanese company 420,000 Japanese yen. The Telephone Company refused to accept the judgment and appealed. The East Asia Development Company also applied for a preliminary attachment on the assets of the Telephone Company. The Shandong High Court has now ruled that the Telephone Company is not responsible for repaying the debt and rejected the East Asia Development Company's application for a preliminary attachment. The Shandong High Court's ruling on the East Asia Development Company's application for a preliminary attachment is recorded below. Shandong High Court Civil Ruling, 20th Year, Complaint No. 245. Ruling Transcript: Applicant, Masakawa Kagawa; Agent, Shin Yoshida. The above applicant and the Jinan Telephone Company are involved in a lawsuit regarding guarantee debt. The court rules as follows on the application for preliminary attachment: "Ruling:" The application is rejected. The application fees shall be borne by the applicant. "Reasons:" According to the provisions of Article 627, Paragraph 1, of the Civil Procedure Law, a preliminary attachment may be applied for to preserve compulsory execution in cases of claims other than claims for money. According to this provision, the subject matter of the claim requested by the parties must be a non-monetary payment in order to apply for a preliminary attachment. This is very clear. In this case, the applicant and the Jinan Telephone Company are involved in a lawsuit regarding guarantee debt. The applicant is requesting that the Telephone Company be jointly and severally liable for repaying the guarantee debt. As for the various assets of the company listed in the application for preliminary attachment, they are not within the scope of the subject matter of the claim in this case. Since the subject matter of the applicant's claim in this case is a claim for money and not a claim for non-monetary payment, the application for preliminary attachment is legally inadmissible. Based on the above conclusion, the application in this case should be deemed illegal. According to Articles 118 and 97 of the same regulation, this ruling is specially made as stated in the main text. Presiding Judge of the Second Civil Division of the Shandong High Court, Yu Jianshu; Judge Yi Xin; Judge Ding Yikui. (June 25th)

French Airplane Arrives in Shenyang via Russia 84

Officials Sent to Inspect Upon Landing

Will Transfer from Shenyang to Beiping, Nanjing, and Shanghai

Shenyang Dispatch: French aviator Cibu, accompanied by his wife and technician Dame, arrived in Shenyang at 12:00 noon on the 24th in a Renault monoplane and landed at the northeast airfield of the Aviation Army. At that time, French Consul Ge Libang in Shenyang greeted them at the scene. The Aviation Headquarters, the Diplomatic Commissioner's Office, and the Shenyang Customs Superintendent's Office also sent personnel to the scene to conduct an inspection and found no prohibited items. Then, the Asia Petroleum Company prepared a heavy truck and loaded thirty barrels of gasoline into the plane. After that, Cibu, his wife, and Dame went to the Yamato Hotel to rest. They are scheduled to fly to Beiping this morning. The plane's load capacity is 2,200 kilograms, its horsepower is 3,000, its capacity is 5 people, and its speed is 240 kilometers per hour. The front of the plane has the national emblems of eleven countries that it has traveled to, the earliest being in 1928. The Northeast Aviation Headquarters also marked a badge on it as a memento. It is reported that Mr. and Mrs. Cibu's trip to China is of a recreational nature. They departed from Paris, the French capital, on the 16th of the month. After landing in Moscow for one day, they were delayed due to strong winds in the White Sea area within the Russian flight line. When flying over Zhazalanor, they planned to fly to the Xing'an area, but turned back midway due to bad weather and flew to Manzhouli. Because the Manzhouli airfield was too small, they did not land and continued to fly to Harbin. However, the airfield there was inconvenient due to the presence of railway lines and crops on all sides, so they did not land there either. They specially flew to Shenyang at 7:30 AM on the 24th and plan to determine their itinerary after arriving in Beiping, Nanjing, and Shanghai. They plan to stay in Beiping for a month. (June 24th)

Citizens of Qingpu County Petition to Prohibit Mining on Jiufeng Mountain 85

Eleven citizens of Qingpu County, Jiangsu Province, including Ni Zhu-hua, He Pei-cang, Qian Yang-qiao, Ni Chang-geng, and He Wei-qin, petitioned to prohibit mining on Jiufeng Mountain. The petition stated: "Petition for the sake of the scenic Jiufeng Mountain, requesting a strict order to prohibit stone quarrying to preserve historical sites and maintain public safety. The Jiufeng Mountains are located between Qingpu and Songjiang. Sheshan, Xueshan, Chenshan, Fenghuangshan, and Kugongshan belong to Qingpu County, while Hengshan, Jishan, Xiaokunshan, and Tianmashan belong to Songjiang County. There are countless tombs of local worthies, ancestral shrines of famous officials, and records of these in the Qingpu and Songjiang County Chronicles since the Tang and Song dynasties. As for the graves of the common people, they are built along the mountains. Everywhere you look, they regard this as a sacred place. For generations, they have all regarded it as a scenic spot. Since the Republic of China, some locals have coveted the mountain stones and secretly obtained mining permits. Although the people of Qingpu and Songjiang have petitioned to prohibit this, one after another, they are digging graves and quarrying stones. Chenshan and Hengshan started first, followed by Xueshan, and then Tianmashan and East Sheshan. It is said that the other mountains, such as Fenghuangshan, Xiaokunshan, Kugongshan, and Jishan, will also be opened for mining. The local villagers are shocked and dare not say anything. The local officials turn a blind eye and conceal the matter, resulting in stone quarries opening in competition, like swarms of bees rising up. If they are allowed to run rampant, the scenic Jiufeng Mountain will inevitably be exhausted by quarrying. Not only will the residents of Qingpu and Songjiang lack a place to mourn and游览, but the millions of people gathered in Shanghai will also suddenly lose a place to enjoy the scenery, relax, and nourish their spirits. The petitioners, Zhu-hua and others, for the sake of the scenic Jiufeng Mountain and for the sake of local public safety, must point out the most obvious harms and report them to your department for your detailed consideration: (1) The Jiufeng Mountains are located in Qingpu and Songjiang, adjacent to Shanghai, and are a place for the people of Songjiang and Shanghai to relax and游览. In the future, when the late Premier Sun Yat-sen's Great Shanghai Plan is realized and the population of Shanghai becomes even denser, the beauty of the mountains and rivers will be even more necessary for tourists to rest. Looking around the civilized countries of the modern world, the opening of parks and the embellishment of mountains and rivers cost millions upon millions each year. Officials are appointed to manage them in order to cultivate the people's character, strengthen their bodies, and achieve their plans to protect the country and strengthen the race. This is common everywhere. However, Shanghai, where millions of people gather, lacks the beauty of parks and the splendor of mountains and rivers. Those with knowledge consider this a regret. Therefore, these only remaining Jiufeng Mountains are not cherished and are allowed to be destroyed by others. Although quarrying stones can generate profits for a time, the destruction of scenic spots, which are used to comfort the mind and body, will erode along with it. The price is not comparable to the mere material benefits. For the sake of the physical and mental cultivation of the majority of the people, we must strongly request preservation. (2) The ancient sites of the Jiufeng Mountains, recorded in the chronicles, all have historical significance, such as the tombs of local worthies, ancestral shrines of famous officials, steles, and memorial arches, which are as precious as the monuments, towers, and bronze statues of Europe and America. Therefore, the Ministry of Interior promulgated the Regulations on the Preservation of Scenic Spots, Historical Sites, and Cultural Relics in September of the 17th year of the Republic of China, stipulating in Articles 2 and 8 that protection should be spared no effort. Once the mountains are opened for stone quarrying, the historical sites will inevitably be destroyed. For the sake of future generations to admire the sages and for the sake of historical research, we must strongly request preservation. (3) There are no less than hundreds of thousands of people's graves in the Jiufeng Mountains. Every year, the descendants sweep the graves, following the tradition. Once they are destroyed and dug up, not only will the corpses be exposed, causing the dead to hate in the underworld, but the living will weep blood and break their hearts, causing unbearable pain. Who has no parents? Who is not a descendant? Even if they are not the descendants of the hundreds of thousands of grave owners in the mountains, who can bear to see this cruelty? Filial piety is our country's inherent morality. The late Premier Sun Yat-sen, in his sixth lecture on nationalism, strongly advocated preservation, saying, "If we can explain the meaning of filial piety to the extreme, the country can naturally become strong." For the sake of maintaining the hard work of the philosophers who have governed the world with filial piety for thousands of years, we must strongly request preservation. (4) Stone quarries are everywhere, with hundreds of small workers in each factory and thousands in ten factories. These workers are of mixed quality, leading to rampant thieves in neighboring villages, causing unrest among the people. For the sake of local security, we must strongly request a ban. (5) The irrigation of farmland near the Jiufeng Mountains relies entirely on mountain water. Now, due to the impact of the opening of the mountains, the mountain water sources are being blocked. This not only hinders water conservancy and farmland, but also the dust from crushing and transporting stones will inevitably spread to the nearby fields. As this accumulates over time, the soil will become solid, and good farmland will turn into stony fields. The fertile land around Jiufeng is no less than hundreds of thousands of acres. In the future, the reduction of agricultural products is inevitable. For the sake of the people's livelihood and national taxes, we must strongly request a ban. In summary, the five harms mentioned above may be difficult for your department to hear about due to the hard work of construction, but the petitioners have witnessed the situation firsthand and dare not suppress the facts. Therefore, we dare to enumerate the harms and respectfully request your department to take into consideration the scenic Jiufeng Mountain and quickly prohibit stone quarrying. All stone quarries should be closed immediately. If there are any who disobey the orders overtly but comply secretly, the people should be allowed to report them, and they should be severely punished according to the law, so as to appease the public and eliminate hidden dangers. This is truly a public benefit. Respectfully submitted."

Local News 86

Qingpu

Rural Woman Abused and Commits Suicide by Arson: In Henggang Village, a subordinate area of the county, the daughter-in-law of Zhong Fulan, surnamed Mou, was constantly abused by her husband. She attempted suicide by poisoning several times, but was always discovered and saved. One morning, while the family was working in the fields, she suddenly locked the room door, piled clothes on the bed, poured kerosene, and then lay down in the bed and set it on fire. Instantly, the fire blazed to the sky, making it impossible to approach. Neighbors heard the alarm and rushed to rescue her, but the fire had already broken through the roof. By the time her family received the news and returned, the house had been completely burned down, and the woman's body was charred black. The whole family wept bitterly, a truly tragic scene.

Shameless Adulteress Murders Her Lover: Near Songjia Mound in the Eleventh District, a farmer named Zhang Laosi began living with a widow named Zhu Abao after his wife died. They lived together as husband and wife. Zhu had a daughter whom Zhang's eldest son married, making them relatives. However, Abao was naturally promiscuous and recently found a new lover. She abandoned her old love for the new, completely changing her previous affectionate demeanor. She repeatedly provoked discord between her son-in-law and his father. The other day, Zhang and his son got into a fight, and Abao helped the son, ultimately killing Laosi. Afterwards, she hung the body from a beam, hoping to cover up the crime. Fortunately, Zhang's second son ran to a neighbor for help, who reported it to the Xujing Public Security First Sub-station. The police were dispatched to arrest the murderer and take her into custody for temporary detention. A written report was prepared and submitted to the county government for an on-site investigation. After the investigation, the suspect and the murder weapon were taken to the county for further investigation.

Suzhou

Lu Shiqiao Acquitted of Official Charges: Lu Shiqiao, a doctor from Beishang Township, Wuxi, along with Bao Dayuan, Guo Asi, Zhu Ada, Lu Genhu, and others, were involved in the case of inciting the shooting of Tan Qixuan, the director of the Administrative Bureau. They appealed to the High Court against the judgment of the Wuxi County Government. After several months of review by Judge Li of the Second Criminal Division of the High Court, a final decision was reached recently. Yesterday (the 27th), the verdict was announced in court. Lu Shiqiao's original death sentence was overturned, and he was declared innocent. Bao Dayuan's original sentence of 20 years imprisonment was upheld, and his appeal was rejected. The original sentences of one year and six months imprisonment for Guo Asi, Lu Genhu, and Zhu Ada were overturned, and they were sentenced to five years imprisonment. It was also advised that if they disagreed with the verdict, they could appeal to the court within ten days after receiving the judgment.

Anti-Banditry Unit Executes Kidnappers: Kidnappers Wang Cihong and Guan Yehua had repeatedly kidnapped an old man from Henggu Township, obtaining 3,400 yuan, and Ma Wenxiang from Xishan, obtaining 4,000 yuan. They also committed robberies in various townships such as Wangjiadang, about ten li southwest of Wujiang Wulu. At the beginning of this month, they went to Nanxun, Zhejiang, to commit robberies. They were captured by the Nanxun Public Security Bureau and the Wuxian Public Security Bureau was notified to send police to escort them back. After a thorough investigation, they were transferred to the Anti-Banditry Command in Suzhou and Zhejiang for disposition. After a thorough review by the military judge, Commander Zhu ordered their execution yesterday (the 27th). At 3 PM, the bandits Wang Cihong and Guan Yehua were brought out, their ages and origins were verified, and they were escorted to the Wangshudun execution ground on Hengma Road for execution by firing squad.

Various Industries Prepay Business Tax: The Wuxian Business Tax Collection Bureau is scheduled to begin collecting taxes today (the 28th). Various industries held a joint meeting at the County Chamber of Commerce yesterday (the 27th) to discuss the procedures. As a result, it was decided that for businesses in the urban area that had joined the trade associations, those with a tax rate of two per thousand would pay one quarter of the total amount of 50,000 yuan, which is 12,500 yuan, first. The Chamber of Commerce would notify them to submit the payment to the Collection Bureau by July 1st. Businesses that had not joined the trade associations and those in various townships, totaling 20,000 yuan, would be collected by the Bureau itself. It is said that the Bureau will send personnel to begin collecting taxes on the 29th.

Request to Abolish Special Tax on Water Pumps: The 17 autonomous district public offices in Wuxi County have been unable to secure funds since the abolition of the cocoon tax, which previously included an autonomous fee. They jointly decided to levy a special tax on water pumps used for irrigation in various townships, one yuan per machine per month, to make up for the shortfall. This has been submitted to the county government and then to the provincial government for discussion at the provincial administrative meeting. Upon hearing this news, the Water Pump Industry Association believed that water pumps were the only agricultural tool for farmers to cultivate their land, which could increase agricultural production, and that it would be difficult to collect a special tax. They submitted a separate petition to the Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining, requesting an exemption from the tax to show compassion. Yesterday, they received a reply from the provincial government, ordering the county government to investigate and review the matter.

Various Recent Rumors About the Opium Monopoly: After the opium monopoly was established, the sales quota for Wuxi was initially 25,000 taels per month. Many people were vying for the position of Director of the Inspection and Suppression Office. However, the monthly sales quota was soon changed to 50,000 taels, causing many people to withdraw. Director Feng, believing that Wuxi was a well-known and desirable position in Suzhou and Changzhou, wondered why no one was interested. After investigating the situation, he reduced the quota to 40,000 taels per month and appointed Wang Zhiliang as the director of the Wuxi branch. Wang, also known as Wang Jiyu, is from Suzhou and currently serves as a staff officer in the Wusong Fortress Command. It is also said that Guo Cifen has been appointed in Wujin, Jiang Xiaodi in Suzhou, Yu Gongcai in Changshu, and Lei Chunsheng in Wujiang.

Gunfire Between Military and Bandits at Gaopukou: At 1 AM on the 26th, five or six bandit ships were spotted at the Gaopukou sea port in this county. The news was reported to the garrison provincial army at Hupukou, the Fifth Sub-station of the Sixth Branch Bureau, and the Police Brigade. A platoon of soldiers led by platoon leader Xi Junfu of the garrison army went to Gaopukou and immediately encountered gunfire from the bandits. After about an hour, the bandits gradually became unsustainable, and more than ten of them carried weapons and landed ashore, disappearing. The soldiers and police also landed and ambushed, intending to capture the bandits when they returned to the ship. About two hours later, another bandit ship arrived and shone a flashlight, spotting the ambush. They exchanged gunfire again, and the bandits abandoned the ship and fled.

On the 26th, the rickshaw pullers fully resumed work and paid the fees and obtained licenses as required. Yongpu Ship Robbed in Xunjiansi Waters: The Yongpu ship, which operates between Shipu in Xiangshan County and Haiyou in Tai County, sailed from Shipu to Haiyou on the lower ninth day of this month and returned to Shipu on the same day. Unexpectedly, two or thirty bandits, dressed in uniforms and posing as military police, mingled among them. The ship's police and crew did not pay attention to them at first, thinking they were military police being transferred. When the ship reached the Xunjiansi waters, the bandit leader gave a signal to carry out the robbery. They first confiscated the ship's police's guns and locked them in the cabin, preventing them from making a sound. Then, they sent bandits to the steering house with the ship's police's guns to monitor the captain, ordering him to sail east. Then, they carried out a large-scale search, and no one on the ship was spared. It is estimated that several hundred yuan in cash and coins were robbed from the accounting room, and the gold and silver ornaments, clothes, and goods of the passengers were robbed for no less than ten thousand yuan. After searching for four days, the captain begged them to release the ship on the 22nd. Before leaving, they kidnapped more than ten passengers. After the ship arrived in Shipu, it has reported to the county government for the military and police to rescue.

On the one hand, they are excavating ground pools in the Jiangjiang area of Toupengdong Longxing Pagoda to make marks. They are also digging up rice seedlings on the cotton fields and building three rectangular ground pools about two feet deep, each covering about one mu of cotton land, to be used as marks.

Strange Sheep Born in Nansha: Zhang Mingqing, a farmer in Xiaosibu, Nansha, has a ewe that gave birth to a lamb on the 20th. It is neither a sheep nor a human. It is more than a foot long, has two legs, a human face, no hands on the upper body, ears like a human, and white fur all over its body. It sits and stands lively. Zhang Zhaofa from Xiaosibu spent twelve yuan to buy the sheep in order to display it in major ports in Shanghai and Hangzhou for public exhibition.

Educational News Highlights

Legislative Yuan Yesterday Revised and Passed the Ministry of Education Organizational Law 87

The Legislative Yuan at its 148th meeting on the 27th revised and passed Articles 20 to 24 of the Ministry of Education Organizational Law as follows:

Article 1: The Ministry of Education manages academic and educational administrative affairs nationwide. Article 2: The Ministry of Education has the responsibility to instruct and supervise the highest-level administrative officials in local areas in the execution of their assigned affairs.

Article 3: The Ministry of Education, regarding its assigned affairs, may request the Premier of the Executive Yuan to submit any orders or [decisions] of the highest-level administrative officials in local areas that it deems to violate laws or exceed their authority to the State Council for deliberation and resolution, after which they may be suspended or revoked.

Article 4: The Ministry of Education establishes the following departments and offices: (1) General Affairs Department (2) Higher Education Department (3) General Education Department (4) Social Education Department (5) Mongolian-Tibetan Education Department (6) Compilation and Examination Office.

Article 5: The Ministry of Education may establish various committees when necessary, the organization of which shall be determined separately.

Article 6: The Ministry of Education, with the approval of the State Council and the Legislative Yuan, may add, merge, or eliminate various departments, offices, and other agencies.

Article 7: The General Affairs Department is responsible for the following matters: (1) receiving, distributing, drafting, correcting, and preserving documents; (2) publishing ministerial orders; (3) guarding seals; (4) recording the entry and exit of staff; (5) compiling statistics and reports; (6) compiling and issuing public announcements; (7) budgeting, settling accounts, and accounting for the Ministry's expenses; (8) managing the Ministry's official property; (9) managing the Ministry's official property; (10) managing the Ministry's general affairs and other matters not belonging to other departments.

Article 8: The Higher Education Department is responsible for the following matters: (1) university education and specialized education; (2) studying abroad; (3) guiding various academic institutions; (4) granting degrees; (5) other higher education matters.

Article 9: The General Education Department is responsible for the following matters: (1) secondary education, primary education, and early childhood education; (2) teacher training; (3) vocational education; (4) establishing and changing local educational institutions; (5) other general education matters.

Article 10: The Social Education Department is responsible for the following matters: (1) mass education and literacy campaigns; (2) supplementary education; (3) education for the disabled and handicapped; (4) aesthetic education; (5) public sports; (6) libraries and preserving documents; (7) other social education matters.

Article 11: The Mongolian-Tibetan Education Department is responsible for the following matters: 1. investigating education in Mongolian and Tibetan regions; 2. establishing various educational undertakings in Mongolian and Tibetan regions; 3. training teachers for Mongolian and Tibetan education; 4. awarding scholarships to Mongolian and Tibetan students; 5. planning education expenses for Mongolian and Tibetan education; 6. other Mongolian and Tibetan education matters.

Article 12: The Compilation and Examination Office compiles and translates books, examines educational books, instruments, and other educational supplies; its organization shall be determined separately.

Article 13: The Ministry of Education establishes a University Committee to resolve important national education and academic matters in accordance with the organizational regulations of the University Committee; the organizational regulations of the University Committee shall be determined separately.

Article 14: The Ministry of Education establishes an Overseas Chinese Education Design Committee to manage matters related to the design of overseas Chinese education; its organizational regulations shall be determined separately.

Article 15: The Minister of Education manages all affairs of the Ministry, supervises subordinate officials and agencies.

Article 16: The Political Vice Minister and the Administrative Vice Minister of Education assist the Minister in handling the affairs of the Ministry.

Article 17: The Ministry of Education establishes four to six secretaries, who are responsible for ministerial meetings and matters assigned by superiors.

Article 18: The Ministry of Education establishes two to four counselors to draft and review laws and orders related to the Ministry.

Article 19: The Ministry of Education establishes five directors to manage the affairs of each department.

Article 20: The Ministry of Education establishes four to six supervisors to inspect and guide educational affairs nationwide.

Article 21: The Ministry of Education establishes fourteen to eighteen section chiefs and eighty to one hundred and ten staff members, who, under the command of superiors, manage the affairs of each section.

Article 22: The Minister of Education is specially appointed, the Vice Ministers, Counselors, Directors, and two Secretaries are selected for simplified appointment, two Supervisors are selected for simplified appointment, Section Chiefs are recommended for appointment, and staff members are appointed.

Article 23: The Ministry of Education's procedural rules are determined by ministerial order.

Article 24: This law shall take effect from the date of its promulgation.

Acting President Shen Siliang Reports

American Van Lien defeated Bowser (France) in front of thousands of spectators today by a score of 6-2, 1-6, 6-2, 6-1 in the fourth week. The audience was the largest in recent days, with the sun shining brightly and the central group surrounded.

Sharp's Failure Regretted by the English 101

In the eyes of the English, the most regrettable thing was the defeat of Sharp, who had previously shown power, in the fourth week. He met Hughes of his own country. Sharp initially won the first set, and Hughes wavered. Sharp's heavy shots from the baseline in the first set were like a machine. Sears's cannonball serve in the second set surprised O'Leary, and he only knew when the ball touched his racket. Wood fought hard for four sets to defeat Manfolo by a score of 6-3, 10-12, 10-8, 6-4. Van Lien's victory over Bowser was entirely due to his cannonball serves and heavy forehand shots, which Bowser could not return, and many wild balls led to his defeat. Bowser's backhand shots were very good.

Boorotra Forfeits Doubles 103

Bowser forfeited doubles today to Machin (USA) and Lantre (France) due to Boorotra's departure from England.

Free Talk

A Word 109

— Qiu Shui

Those without money speak of optimism; the cowardly speak of humanitarianism. Diplomats from weak countries speak of justice. Those who are suppressed and have nowhere to complain speak of the law.

Those who laugh easily have no sympathy; those who cry easily have no courage.

If you don't say something that can excite people in this world, then people will never pay attention to you. Because people in the world will never pay attention to things that have nothing to do with themselves.

A fool's brain can digest philosophy into foolishness, science into superstition, and art into pedantry.

Our ideals are like the ancient Shinto gods, constantly requiring people's sacrifices.

If a person loves education, criminal law, and sports, he can become a completely modern gentleman as long as he has money.

Social problems seem complicated, but in reality, there are only two topics: one is how to make the poor rich, and the other is how to make the rich useful to society.

When you read the biographies of famous people, you must remember that the truth is never worth publishing.

There is only one kind of child in society who doesn't want to eat candy, and that is the apprentice in a candy store. So the angels themselves never hope for happiness to come.

Love of fame and greed for profit are the root of all evils.

Tan Yunshan Returns from Touring Tibet and India 110

— Wan Cheng

At 6:00 PM on June 23rd, I accompanied Mr. Huang Jingwan to visit Mr. Tan Yunshan, who had returned from touring Tibet and India. The following is a record of the conversation.

Mr. Tan Yunshan previously served as a Chinese professor at the International University founded by the great Indian poet Tagore. In the winter of the 19th year of the Republic, he went to Tibet from Myanmar to investigate the culture and religion of Tibet. On April 1st of this year, he returned to India from Tibet and toured various Buddhist sites and major cities in India, east, west, north, and south, to investigate Buddhist traces. His travel companions included Mr. Liu Xiunan, the principal of the Zunkong Middle School in Shanghai, and the Daojie Master. They visited Bodh Gaya, the place where the Buddha attained enlightenment, Lingjiu Mountain, the place where the Buddhas preached, Nalanda, the place where the Sanzang Master obtained scriptures, Deer Park, the place where the Buddha turned the wheel of Dharma, Kushinagar, the place where the Buddha entered Nirvana, Nampingni, the place where the Buddha was born, and Shravasti, Jeta Grove Anathapindika Park, the place where the World Honored One preached. They investigated the above-mentioned major holy sites and obtained many commemorative items from the Buddhist country. Furthermore, they passed through Delhi, which was once the capital of India, and visited the imperial palace and the new Delhi Parliament, the Governor's Palace, museums, etc.

Mr. Tan met Gandhi in Batoli, West India, and lived with him for several days. Gandhi got up at 4:00 AM every day and walked until 5:30 AM. One morning, Gandhi planned to invite Mr. Tan to go for a walk, but Tan was sleeping soundly, and Gandhi did not wake him up. Later, Gandhi said to Tan, "I have come several times, but you are always asleep." Tan replied, "Why didn't you wake me up?" Gandhi replied, "You worked hard yesterday and should sleep a few more hours." His respect for people's freedom and love was like this.

Gandhi often goes to the countryside and receives enthusiastic cheers from the people. The people raise money and give gifts to Gandhi. Children come to touch his head and feet to express their affection. Gandhi is also gentle like a "lamb." Poor people have no money to buy gifts, so they give him the yarn they spun themselves. His personality has influenced the people of the country like this.

Mr. Tan is from Chaling, Hunan. He recently returned to China and arrived in Shanghai. He will leave for Beijing soon.

Record of the Big Sword Society in Yuxi Bay, Fujian 111

— Chen Hui

During the late Qing Dynasty, the Yihetuan used sorcery to create chaos in the Central Plains, causing resentment among foreigners. They eventually brought about the disaster of the Allied Forces, which led to the almost complete destruction of the capital, the emperor and empress fleeing, paying reparations, and ceding land, leaving our country with great shame in history. The people of the country still mourn it today. The Big Sword Society in Yuxi Bay, Fujian, recently has a technique similar to that of the Yihetuan. I am writing this to inform the people of the country.

The Big Sword Society is a group formed by the villagers of Yuxi to defend against bandits. There are many bandits in the upper reaches of Fujian. After the defeat of the rebels, their subordinates had no home to return to, and some returned to their original nature and became bandits again. As a result, the people of northern Fujian were trapped deeper and deeper in the water and fire. Yuxi, which was known for its tranquility, was also ravaged. The villagers suffered from this, so they recruited strong men to form the Big Sword Society for self-defense. The leader of the team is from Jiangxi and has a magical technique that can use spells to defend against guns and cannons. During battle, he swallows several pieces of paper with spells on them and sticks them on his chest. They agree not to open their mouths, otherwise, the spells will not work. When bandits come with guns, they do not move at all. When cannons come, they faint slightly and then recover. Therefore, the bandits are defeated. On weekdays, they live in various places and engage in their own businesses. When the alarm sounds, they gather together. Their weapons are big swords, not guns or cannons. Therefore, they are called the Big Sword Society. The team's discipline is very strict. Those who are addicted to smoking and alcohol are not allowed to join the team. Those who are greedy for money are not allowed to join the team. Those who have been bandits are also not allowed to join the team. I heard this from a guest from Yuxi, so I can say it with certainty.

Reading Idle Talk 112

— Ms. Qiyun

I love reading novels the most. Once I have a book in hand, I forget to sleep and eat. But I think that no matter whether it is a Chinese or foreign novel, it is better to appreciate the twists and turns of the plot than to appreciate the beauty of the writing. Therefore, I dare to say that "The Romance of the Western Chamber" is not as good as "Dream of the Red Chamber," "Romance of the Three Kingdoms" is not as good as "Water Margin," and even "All Quiet on the Western Front" is not as good as "The Good Earth." "Resurrection" is not as good as "Plum Blossom Falling." Although the criticism from a literary standpoint is not like this, from the standpoint of my reading interest, I always feel that the more twists and turns in the plot, the better.

I once read a novel called "Red Tear Shadow." I felt that its plot was more tortuous than any book I had ever read. It wrote about "a rich young master who fell in love with a poor girl. Because society and the family could not sympathize with their marriage, they had to go to a foreign country and live a secret life. Later, the rich young master inherited the inheritance and returned home. He entrusted the woman to an old woman. At this time, the woman had already given birth to a pearl in her palm, but she died of sorrow and anger. After the rich young master returned, he was almost forced to marry another woman. Unexpectedly, that wife also suddenly died of illness. So he vowed never to marry again. He also went to the old woman to take back his daughter. But the old woman had bad intentions and replaced his daughter with her own daughter, instead treating his daughter as her own. The old woman's daughter was a heartless, extravagant, and promiscuous person, but his own daughter was very quiet and chaste. Therefore, several strange dramas were created. Later, the rich young master wanted to recruit a son-in-law for his daughter. Who knew that the young man did not love his daughter (actually the old woman's daughter) but fell in love with the old woman's daughter (actually the rich young master's true daughter), and a murder almost occurred. Later, the old woman's conscience was discovered, and she revealed the secret. Only then did the truth come out." The twists and turns of its plot, my law is really unable to describe its ten thousandth. I think this novel is really the most beloved by me to read. Now it is said that the Mingxing Film Company has already made it into the "Red Tear Shadow" film. Then, the power of performance on the screen must be much more ingenious than what is described in the book.

Tidbits 113

— (Juan)

You don't have to pursue love, because sometimes it will grow wings and fly, and grow legs and run. If you don't pursue love, it may come to find you on its own.

Travels in India (52) 114

— Linghua

19th. Many Muslim professors and students know Persian. Talk to me about Persian affairs. And said that the ancient Persian Manichaeism spread to China. I asked if Manichaeism still exists today. Answered no. According to them, the ancient Muslim king was in trouble with Manichaeism and wrote to China. The Chinese king replied. I am also willing to trouble the Manichaeans. Not allowed in China. I don't know if this is true. It should be between the Tang and Song dynasties. Communication between Persia and China is quite difficult to examine. According to the current location of the Biography of King Mu of Zhou, it is said that King Mu of Zhou traveled west and married the Queen Mother of the West, and the scenery in the Biography of King Mu is now the Persian capital of Isfahan. Jiang Guanyun's Examination of the Chinese Race also said that foreign books said that King Xiang had married the Persian Queen. Originally, the lack of communication between the East and the West was due to the isolation of the Muslim countries. And whether there were two kings marrying in ancient China. Gu Jiang also advocated his theory. I am now asking my Muslim friends who study Persian history. It is also difficult to understand. I intend to ask the Persians.

20th, I accidentally met a Chinese merchant in the market. One is surnamed Li. One is surnamed Huang. They

are shoe merchants. According to them, there are three families in this market. Their whole family has lived here for decades. There are many shoe stores in central India. Because Indians lack this manufacturing. Soon I saw six or seven Chinese people coming here. They said they came from Lucknow. Today is the Lunar New Year's Day. So come and visit. But I see their entertainment life. All are playing cards. Because I think the Chinese people are generally like this everywhere. It is also a major shortcoming of the Chinese people. He is the highest person in the education sector. And also loves gambling. Asked me the reason. I can only say it is a habit. Also, a friend of the educator talked about this. They study the principle of gambling. It is also very difficult to cancel. I think this is also a kind of competitive nature. It has become a habit for a long time. Connecting the corners and decorating them on the wall made me feel quite uneasy. It's okay to take only the corners. Even its head is not elegant.

The Tragic Tale of Orchid and Iris 115

— Jing Mengdie

West of Lanling, there is the Wangxian Bridge. It is said that Ding Lingwei passed through here when he transformed into a crane and returned. The residents by the bridge have long formed a market. In one of the families, surnamed Zhu, three daughters were born. The eldest was named Ying (Oriole), the second Feng (Phoenix), and the third Yan (Swallow). Ying was married early but was not happy in her husband's family. This was not due to a romantic entanglement like Wang Lang's regret, but because she was a fierce woman, unable to serve her in-laws, even resorting to violence. The neighbors could not tolerate her, and after years of litigation that remained unresolved, she often resided at her mother's home, accompanying her sister in her boudoir and confiding in Feng. She spoke at length about the misfortunes of women getting married, using her own experiences as a cautionary tale. She employed her eloquent tongue to expound on the merits of remaining single, trying to persuade Feng to embrace spinsterhood. Through repeated praises and heartfelt pleadings, day and night, Feng was eventually swayed and desired to remain a maiden forever. The two elders in the family were oblivious to this. When the autumn of last year approached, Feng's wedding day drew near, but she remained steadfast in her sister's teachings. When the bridal sedan arrived at the door, she covered her face and wept against the wall. Her parents and relatives tried to persuade her, but she refused to yield. However, at the last moment, she broke her promise, delaying the auspicious occasion. How could the matchmaker explain this to the go-between? They tried to persuade her for a long time but to no avail, and were forced to negotiate with the youngest daughter, Yan, scheming to substitute her like a plum for a peach, a plan to graft a new flower onto the tree. Yan readily agreed and, after dressing up, boarded the sedan. On their wedding night, the groom, upon inquiring about the reason at the bedside, was deeply moved by her affection and showed her even greater love and respect. From then on, whenever Yan returned home, she always brought her new husband. Like a pair of mandarin ducks or inseparable fish, they were always together. Feng, however, remained a maiden living at home, without a husband, and her age was increasing. Seeing a perfect match being given away to her younger sister for no reason, she felt regret. Whenever she encountered Yan and her husband, she felt both shame and jealousy. As a result, the once close sisters became like Yin and Xing, avoiding each other. Ying was still unaware of the situation. One day, seeing Feng talking about the love between Yan and her husband, she laughed and said, "It's only like that in the beginning of a marriage. The regrets of the future will be just like mine." Feng scoffed at her, saying, "Sister, enough! How can you still not see that your actions were your own fault, and claim that all married women in the world are like you?" Ying could not endure this and responded with harsh words. From then on, the sisters became enemies, not exchanging a single word with each other. Those neighbors who knew about this all said that Ying had misguided herself and others, and pitied Feng's empty boudoir and lonely figure, a mistake that could never be undone. The autumn moon and spring breeze only deepened her eternal regret. It is said that she has recently become afflicted with madness. Alas, women are prone to deep emotions, and beautiful women often have short lives. Fair faces turn into yellow earth, a matter of time. A case like Feng's is just another in the world of love, resentment, and suffering.

Novel Supporting Society

??? (5) 116

— Xu Zhuodai

Ziliang first divided the hundred or so composition books. Because these were for three grades, there were also three topics. He first separated them into three stacks, then took one from the first grade stack and began to look it over, intending to start writing. Suddenly, he heard a sound from the back door. The maid had gone out to buy groceries, and his wife was calling from downstairs:

"Ziliang!"

Ziliang deliberately didn't answer, knowing that she didn't have anything important. If he answered her, she would just keep bothering him.

"Ziliang! Come down here!"

Pan Ziliang first scooped some water from the water bowl onto the inkstone, rubbed the ink a few times, and then went to find a brush, but it wasn't on his desk.

"Ziliang! Why aren't you answering?"

Where could a brush have gone? Ziliang thought carefully and remembered. He had seen her drawing patterns on shoe uppers with it yesterday, it must be his brush. Ziliang hurried to the front room and searched in a sewing rattan box on the windowsill, and sure enough, he found a goat-hair brush.

"Ziliang! Are you asleep? Are you sleepwalking?"

She heard footsteps on the floorboards upstairs and said this deliberately. When Ziliang returned to the attic room, he heard someone knocking on the door. Yueru went to open the door. Ziliang squatted down and looked out from the small wooden openings above the wall in the sitting room, and saw that it was a mailman who had come in after the door was opened. Ziliang sat down to do his own work.

As soon as the front door closed, Yueru rushed upstairs again. Ziliang saw her holding a large envelope.

"Wang Renfu's father has died, the obituary has arrived."

Saying this, she handed the obituary to Ziliang. Ziliang took it but didn't look at it, placing it on the table. She said, "His old man had been sick for a long time, and finally he's died. I knew he was going to die a few years ago, now he's finally died, he's really dying for the first time."

His wife looked at Ziliang's desk:

"I called you like I was summoning a ghost, and you didn't answer. So, you were here correcting compositions. Good! Good! I'll write an article too, and ask you to correct it for me!"

Financial and Gold Prices Plummet Violently 117

Plummeting Eighteen Taels and Six Mace

Heavily Breaching the 700-Tael Mark Yesterday, the plunge in gold prices intensified drastically, with the 700-tael mark being breached again. The massive surge and tidal wave were irresistible. The conditions were unpredictable, and the price fluctuated with a difference of eighteen or nineteen taels. Ultimately, it plummeted by more than twenty taels, causing extreme fear among the industry, like being lost in a fog, with no clear direction. The sudden drop was likely due to the silver market's expected drop not materializing yesterday, resulting in failed reports. Furthermore, the rise in the US stock market served as a catalyst for the Shanghai market. The exchange rate was unusually loose, with a longer spread for postings. Consequently, the gold price had already plummeted by more than ten taels early in the morning. Bullish firms were panicked and inclined to sell off. Subsequently, the weakness intensified, creating a sense of upheaval. It suddenly dropped to 690 taels, and then major players changed their strategy, taking advantage of the low point to buy in, which brought the price back up by more than ten taels. However, in the final situation, the trend was still weak. This morning, the large bar appeared to be rising, likely because it was Saturday afternoon, when the market usually closes.

A Terrible Loss of One Hundred Taels This Week The market this week experienced unprecedented massive changes, influenced by President Hoover's announcement of a moratorium on war debt payments. The highest price at the beginning of the week was 792 taels, and the lowest price on Saturday was 690 taels and 5 mace, a difference of over one hundred taels, which was unexpected. Main Reasons for Last Week's American Cotton Rebound 125

President Hoover's Suggestions War Payment

Industry and Speculative Shorts Strongly Covered

A telegram from New York on the 26th reported on the cotton market during the week: The cotton market last week also turned upward following President Hoover's suggestions for delaying war payments. Industry and speculative shorts actively covered, and supply was limited to the liquidation of old longs and intermittent sales from the South. As a result, the market turned upward, and supplies were ready to be absorbed. Speculators' interest also increased, and the longs who bought due to delayed war payments were further empowered by the activity in the cotton market and the unfavorable news about the new flowers in the South. However, the weather in May and June was favorable, and the current temperature is high, which is likely to severely damage the bollworm. The longs for July continued to liquidate. Recent Flour Prices Drop to Two Liang 127

Yesterday in the flour market, after the morning opening bell, there was once again significant volatility in the prices of various months. Because gold prices plummeted again, and the exchange rate increased daily, the price of foreign flour wheat was bound to gradually fluctuate. Given these circumstances, the thoughts of those inside and outside the industry were naturally affected. Therefore, after opening, the prices for the current month and July fell to two liang, August to two liang and seven and a half li, September to two liang and two and a half fen, October to two liang and four and a half fen, and November to two liang and four li and seven and a half hao, a drop of about two fen compared to the previous day. Afterwards, due to offsetting profits from short positions, there was a slight rebound. By the afternoon opening bell, the market sentiment for each month was generally stable. Because factory selling eased slightly, and mainland buyers were quite active, the situation was held up. However, looking at the future, because the exchange rate is rising and foreign wheat can be ordered step by step, it may be difficult to be optimistic in the future. As a result, the prices for the current month and August and September remained unchanged, July improved slightly by two and a half li, and October and November improved slightly by five and a half li.

Wheat Prices Plunge Before Noon 128

Yesterday, the wheat market presented a plunging trend again in the morning. Because gold prices fell sharply, the combined price of foreign wheat gradually eased. Once this path opened, people's hearts were agitated, and it was exceptionally fierce. Because this kind of environment has been tried repeatedly, it is impossible to skillfully avoid it no matter what. Therefore, although the current month's trading was suspended, prices for July and beyond fell sharply step by step, with a drop of seven, eight, and nine fen compared to the previous day. By the afternoon opening bell, people's hearts seemed slightly more stable. With the flour market weakening and then rebounding, prices for each month showed a slight upward trend. However, traders who were fixing foreign wheat again made several deals. For example, Australian wheat was priced at only four liang and one qian and a half, and Chicago's No. 2 spring wheat was bid at only four liang and six fen. Given this situation, there is indeed a possibility of a heavy fall in the future. As a result, July fell by five fen compared to the previous day, August fell by six fen, September and October fell by five fen, and November fell by seven fen. Spot wheat prices remain weak due to sluggish factory demand, and the asking price for medium and lower quality goods has dropped by another three to five fen. A total of over 1,900 packages of wheat from Kaihuzhou, Wusong, Anting, Nanjing, Penglai, and Yangzhou were handled by Fuxin.

Silk and Tea: Lyon's Shanghai Factories are More Active Due to Demand 129

Yesterday, the local foreign firm silk market became increasingly firm due to the activation of actual sales in Lyon by Shanghai white silk factories. The reason is that French silk factories have a strong demand for autumn silk raw materials, and silk telegrams continue to be transferred to Shanghai. Although transactions are difficult to be smooth, the market sentiment is brisk. Yesterday, Xinfu and others brought in 50 packages of Shanghai white silk factory silk, and Zhonghe brought in 20 packages of Baiqian silk, and the prices remained firm.

New York Raw Silk Opening Prices Rise 130

Since the beginning of summer, the New York market has seen depressed raw silk opening prices due to Japanese silk merchants selling at low prices. Now, because the Japanese government is restricting the production of summer and autumn silkworm cocoons, and spring cocoons have also had a poor harvest, the market price of Yokohama raw silk is rising daily, and the price of New York raw silk is also rising accordingly. The day before yesterday, Grade A opened at $2.90, Grade B at $2.45, and Grade C at $1.90, each rising by 45 cents per pound.

Transactions for Both Black and Green Tea Are Scarce 131

Yesterday, only Jardine Matheson and China Tea Company bought over a hundred boxes of Keemun black tea, and the prices all trended down by over ten taels. The outgoing route for Luzhuang Zhenmei green tea continued to be sluggish. Although local merchants bought 210 boxes of goods through Jinlong Foreign Firm, the market price opened at 52 taels, another four or five taels lower than before. Currently, the sources from various routes are not smooth. The attitudes of Chinese merchants are mostly inconsistent due to tea quotas being short, some firm and some weak. However, broadly speaking, the future cannot be optimistic.

Wuyuan Seed Tea is Eagerly Purchased 132

In Wuyuan County, seed tea has been picked by mountain households for several days, and shipments are very active. However, because trademark owners have not purchased much spring tea, their need is urgent, and demand is quite exceeding supply. Ordinary tea merchants are swarming to search for purchases. Some even hold lamps and sit guarding tea households, forcibly taking the tea as soon as it is roasted, or setting the price in the morning and weighing the tea at night. The intensity of the rush purchases is truly rare. The market price remains firm at 65 to 70 cents per catty, without falling. Mountain households are happy to pick and sell because the price of seed tea is higher than that of first-flush tea. Therefore, the excitement of tea households picking and processing these days is no less than that of first-flush tea. In addition, the tea trees that did not develop enough first-flush tea are sprouting exceptionally densely. Approximately every dan of tea trees can yield 30 catties of seed tea, which is fragrant and thick, and is more than equal to first-flush tea.

Piece Goods: There Are Already Inquiries About Autumn Seasonal Woolens 133

There are many inquiries about the woolens sold in the autumn market, such as "rotten paste" woolen fabric, printed woolen fabric, "maiden" fabric, plain thick woolen fabric, hat woolen fabric, yarn woolen fabric, etc. Local merchants have pre-purchased. It is found that the recent shipments of these woolens from abroad are not many, and each store has ordered less, probably due to the increase in tariffs. Although there are also many old stocks, they are a drop in the bucket and not enough to sell. Therefore, the opening prices are more expensive than other woolens, especially for "rotten paste" woolen fabric and printed woolen fabric. Buyers are also aware of this situation, so many are rushing to purchase in advance, predicting that the selling price will definitely be firmer when they hit the market in the autumn season.

Sugar Market: Raw Sugar and White Sugar Prices Fall and Sales Are Sluggish 134

Yesterday, according to the sugar market telecommunications from the production area, the price of Cuban raw sugar remained unchanged. New York futures sugar for September and May of the next year both fell by two fen, and the other months also fell by one fen each. The current and futures prices of Javanese sugar also had few fluctuations. The association's market allocation saw sluggish buying of Dutch sugar No. 24 raw white sugar, and shipments were quite strong, with the price easing to 11 taels and 2 qian, but inquiries were still scarce. No. 20 medium raw white sugar was at 10 taels and 6 qian, and transactions were also rare. The weakness of the market is truly rare. Although the Japanese sugar market has declined again, imports and exports still feel active. N-mark was at 10 taels and 8 qian, SH-mark at 10 taels and 5 qian and a half, I-mark at 11 taels and 2 qian, YRO-mark at 10 taels and 4 qian and a half, YT-mark at 10 taels and 7 qian and a half, YP-mark at 11 taels and 1 qian and seven and a half fen, old goods at 11 taels and 1 qian, LK-mark at 10 taels and 8 qian, TM-mark at 10 taels and 6 qian and a half, and Taikoo B-mark old goods at 11 taels and 1 qian and seven and a half fen. The market conditions were all stable. Trademark plate transactions were particularly quiet. ARAE Japanese sugar factory plates matched with August and September goods were priced at 4 yuan and 6 jiao in Japanese currency, with slight inquiries. It is heard that a telegram has been sent to the factory, and the price must wait for the factory's reply to be valid.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Held a General Meeting of Members Yesterday 152

Telegram Request to Eliminate the Red Bandits in the Shortest Time

Passed the Principle of Cooperatively Collecting Business Tax in this City

The 20th Annual General Meeting of Members of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce was held in the conference hall yesterday afternoon at 2 PM. Details are recorded as follows:

Meeting Venue Arrangement: The Party and National flags were hung at the entrance of the Chamber and the conference hall. Registration tables were set up outside the hall, divided into left and right groups for signing in. A podium was set up at the front of the hall, with a table for the chairman in front of it. Slogans were posted throughout the hall, including: (1) Merchants can have strength if they unite; (2) Merchants can relieve suffering if they unite; (3) Merchants must unite to resist economic aggression; (4) The general meeting of members should promote the spirit of revolution; (5) Shanghai merchants are the pioneers of world trade wars; (6) Shanghai merchants should be the leaders of international trade.

Meeting Staff: (Chairman Group) Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Ye Huijun, Xu Jilao, Yuan Ludeng; (Secretary) Yan Esheng; (General Manager and Master of Ceremonies) Zheng Chengqing; (Recorder) Nie Desheng, Zhou Songxun; (Reception) Sun Mingqi, Jin Shengbai, Xue Guangqian, Wu Jichun, Huang Zaishi, Zhu Dechao, Sun Feijun, Ren Shoupeng; (Sign-in) Peng Zaizhi, Wang Youshan, Zhang Yukun, Luo Shiying.

Attendees: Those who attended yesterday included Zhu Kui from the Municipal Party Department, Song Zhongqing, representative of the Social Affairs Bureau, and representatives of various trade associations, shops, and members, including the banking industry, money industry, shipping industry, gold industry, silk factory industry, silk and satin industry, bean and rice industry, North-South goods brokerage industry, fur industry, flour mill industry, oil cake industry, jewelry industry, yarn industry, egg industry, sugar industry, book industry, cotton cloth industry, timber industry, coal industry, securities industry, paper industry, and other trade associations, as well as representatives of Sanyou Industrial Society, Jiuda Refined Salt Company, China United Life Insurance Company, Huashang Yizhong Auction House, Securities Exchange, and other shop members, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Gu Xinyi, Cheng Xiechun, Lu Bohong, Xu Jilao, Wu Zhihao, Ma Jiliang, Zhang Shuliang, Yuan Ludeng, Hu Juewen, Wang Lianfang, Fang Jiaobo, Zhu Wenqi, Chen Songyuan, Mao Chunpu, Wen Lanting, Ye Jiaxing, Lu Feibohong, Wang Zhixin, Lu Yuequan, and 259 other people.

Meeting Order: (1) Ringing the bell to start the meeting; (2) All stand; (3) Paying the highest respect to the Party and National flags and the portrait of the Prime Minister; (4) The Chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will (Ye Huijun); (5) Report from the Chairman Group: (A) Report on the number of attendees; (B) Report on the venue (both by Wang Xiaolai); (6) Instructions from representatives of Party and government agencies; (7) Discussion of proposals; (8) Closing remarks by the Chairman (Wang Yansong); (9) Ringing the bell to adjourn the meeting.

Meeting Situation: After the rituals, Chairman Wang Xiaolai reported that as of the start of the meeting, 206 member representatives had attended. Next, he reported on the Chamber's affairs, which were divided into 12 sections: (1) Implementation of the resolutions of the previous general meeting of members; (2) The process of revising the articles of association of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; (3) Guidance and organization of various trade associations; (4) Disputes and review of various industry regulations; (5) Obtaining considerable effects in requesting exemption or reduction of harsh taxes and levies; (6) Handling diplomatic matters; (7) Requesting the elimination of labor-management disputes; (8) Mediation of commercial disputes; (9) Obtaining approval to relocate arbitrarily occupied guild houses; (10) Drafting various regulations of the Chamber; (11) Matters related to the construction of the Chamber: (A) Establishment of a domestic goods bazaar in the commodity exhibition hall; (B) Expansion of the commercial library; (C) Catching up on the overdue publication of the Commercial Monthly; (D) Construction of school buildings for the commercial night school; (E) Establishment of a correspondence class and publication of a correspondence monthly; (12) Contributions to the current situation. After the report, representatives of Party and government agencies gave instructions, and then the discussion of proposals began as follows: (1) Member application for withdrawal from the Chamber: Resolved that Jiangnan Paper Company and Zhufeng Enamel Company members should not be allowed to withdraw, and that the membership of Meihuali Clock and Watch Manufacturing Factory should naturally be terminated because it had been sold; (2) A proposal to add a 30% public debt fund when collecting membership fees: Resolved, passed; (3) A proposal to schedule the repayment of public construction debts from the former General Chamber of Commerce and the former South Shanghai Chamber of Commerce: Resolved, passed; (4) The 19th annual final accounts and the 20th annual budget proposal: Resolved, passed; (5) A proposal to request the government to issue a clear order that all members of the same industry should join the same industry association for unification; (6) A proposal that members of the same industry must join the same industry association, and the same industry association must join the Chamber of Commerce: The above two proposals were discussed together, resolved, and requested the Legislative Yuan and the Ministry of Industry to supplement the articles of association in the detailed rules for the implementation of trade associations; (7) A proposal to request the Stamp Tax Bureau to carefully punish and stipulate the inspection of account books, limited to this year; (8) A proposal to prevent the Stamp Tax Bureau from imposing harsh penalties without limiting the year: The above two proposals were discussed together, resolved, and a letter was sent to the Stamp Tax Bureau; (9) A proposal that the inspection of weights and measures should be carried out jointly by the trade association; (10) The new weights and measures system will be implemented on a regular basis, but if the new instruments cannot be fully issued before the deadline, please forward to the Social Security Bureau and the Public Security Bureau to temporarily postpone the destruction of the old instruments: The above two proposals were discussed together, resolved, and the principle was passed, and the Executive Committee was asked to handle it with discretion; (11) Please submit to the Ministry of Industry to order the provincial and municipal governments that the duties of notaries should be exercised by Chinese merchants: Resolved, submitted to the Ministry of Industry; (12) A proposal from the brick and tile industry to request the financial authorities to exempt the tooth tax because of the unscrupulous plunder of unlicensed brokers: Resolved, forwarded; (13) A proposal to amend the issue of liability for compensation and request the French Concession Board to change the customer signature regulations: Resolved, regarding customer signatures, the original Chinese and foreign texts should prevail, and the Chamber has sent a letter to the French Concession Board of Directors requesting its amendment. Regarding the issue of liability for compensation, since it is a matter of civil law and has great significance, it should be handed over to the Executive Committee for detailed study and further deliberation; (14) The dispute between the brokerage fees of the exchange and herbal medicine gangs has not been resolved for a long time, affecting the Chamber's affairs. Please submit it to the conference for relief: Resolved, handed over to the Executive Committee for detailed investigation, a proper remedy plan was drafted, and submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for adoption; (15) A request to the government to amend the export tariff rules for eggs: Resolved, the Chamber will submit to the National Government to temporarily collect taxes at the old tax rate; (16) The Finance Department of Anhui Province violated the Ministry's order to collect business tax on egg farms, and also violated Article 5 of the supplementary measures of the outline of the business tax, and appointed people to handle the egg tax. How should it be legally stopped: Resolved, and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for correction; (17) The Chamber should quickly produce standard order forms for purchasing goods from foreign merchants and send them to various industries for reference: Resolved, the Executive Committee will formulate them according to the original plan and send them to various industries for reference; (18) The Chamber should quickly handle commercial statistics: Resolved, the Executive Committee should prepare for it as soon as possible; (19) All commercial laws and regulations promulgated by the government and increased donations and taxes must be consulted with the Chamber of Commerce. If accidents related to commerce occur in society, they should also be consulted by the Chamber of Commerce, and when the Chamber of Commerce holds meetings to discuss, it must also convene representatives of the industry to directly participate in the consultation: Resolved, and submitted to the National Government for adoption; (20) The Chamber of Commerce should automatically mediate commercial disputes in various industries, actively investigate the truth, and give fair judgments: Resolved, the Executive Committee should pay attention to handling it at any time; (21) Exporting domestic goods should be tax-free to develop foreign trade: Resolved, and submitted to the National Government; (22) A proposal to revitalize woolen factories and request the Political Council to promote cooperation: Resolved, and submitted to the Ministry of Industry for adoption; (23) A letter from the Business Tax Preparatory Office of the Municipal Finance Bureau, for the convenience of merchants, the business tax in this city is proposed to be paid by the Chamber of Commerce to simplify the process. This case was discussed by the 15th Executive Committee on the 24th of this month. It was agreed that the collection of business tax should be mainly handled by the government, but for the convenience of merchants and to avoid harassment, the Chamber of Commerce can be in a position to cooperate in the collection. The principles should be submitted to the general meeting of members for approval, and the detailed methods should be carefully drafted by the Executive Committee and discussed with the Finance Bureau: Resolved, passed; (24) Please inform the merchants to comply with the order to implement the settlement of accounts at the end of January, May, and September each year and not to delay arbitrarily: Resolved, issue a notice flyer and distribute it to all industries and gangs to comply with; (25) Please ask the government to issue an order to the stamp tax bureaus across the country to promote foreign merchants in the concession to affix stamp tax tickets to show that Chinese and foreigners are treated equally and to enrich tax revenue: Resolved, and submitted to the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to handle; (27) Please send a letter to the Shanghai County Finance Bureau to stop issuing brokerage registration certificates and instead issue business licenses: Resolved, the Executive Committee will send a letter to the Shanghai County Finance Bureau based on the business tax law; (27) It is proposed to amend the business tax rate for the Western clothing industry in this city. Manufacturers should be exempt from business tax in accordance with the precedent of the garment industry, and sellers should be taxed at the same tax rate as the garment industry: Resolved, after review by the Executive Committee, a letter was sent to the Finance Bureau; (28) Telegram to General Commander Chiang to eliminate the Red bandits in the shortest time: Resolved, passed; (30) The industry regulations of various industries that have been reviewed and approved by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce should be submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for approval and record as soon as possible: Resolved, passed, and a letter was sent to the Public Works Department. In the future, the engineering office, fire brigade, and health office of the department should set up special committees and hire as many Chinese employees as possible to eliminate the alienation between Chinese and foreigners and eliminate all disputes: Resolved, passed; (33) Send a letter to the courts and public security bureaus in Shanghai to assist the industry associations in various industries to recover the membership fees owed by members at any time: Resolved, the Executive Committee will handle it with discretion; (33) The Chamber of Commerce should hold a quarterly dinner party for the representatives of the industry associations: Resolved, the Executive Committee will handle it with discretion.

Closing Remarks: Finally, Executive Committee member Wang Yansong gave closing remarks, stating, "Today's conference discussed a total of 33 proposals, including those related to the overall situation, such as the telegram requesting the elimination of the Red bandits, those related to the burden of merchants in the city, such as the passage of the principle of the Chamber of Commerce cooperating in the collection of business tax in the city, and those related to the organization of the association and the suffering of various industries. Such important proposals have yielded satisfactory results in a short period of time, and the enthusiasm and spirit of the representatives are commendable. However, the success of the association's work depends entirely on the stability of the association's basic organization and the efforts of the members of the basic organization. I hope that the industry associations can develop their association affairs and consolidate their foundations. I also hope that the member representatives can use their enthusiasm and perseverance to seek the development of the association's affairs, and the future results will be immeasurable. I will follow the representatives and use the spirit of one mind and one heart to seek continuous progress."

Telegram Requesting the Suppression of Bandits: After the conference closed, a telegram was sent to General Commander Chiang that night, which read, "NanChang sent Chiang General Commander Junjian, festival 麾 visited Gan, supervised the generals, divided the roads and surrounded, the people of the ravaged, all are celebrating. The association held a general meeting of members today, and Gan is the center of the Yangtze River and the southeast overall situation. In recent years, the water is deep and the fire is hot, and it has been in a foreign land for a long time. The lessons of the past are worth learning from. To strengthen the foundation of the country, we must first lay the foundation for the people's livelihood. Therefore, at the general meeting, it was resolved to appeal to your seat in the shortest possible time to supervise and encourage the generals and soldiers to sweep away the bandits and capture the leaders, so that the remaining people can have hope of recovery. We respectfully telegraph to present our situation and await your adoption, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Jiang Zuobin and His Wife Will Go to Mogan Mountain for Recuperation 154

Change of Position is Definitely Not True

Expected to Return to Duty After Autumn Cools Down

Minister to Germany Jiang Zuobin has been on leave and returned to China for many days. Because his wife is weak and sick, he is scheduled to go to Mogan Mountain for summer recuperation on the 30th of this month. Jiang will stay for about a week and then return to Shanghai. He is scheduled to go to Europe in the autumn to return to his post as ambassador to Germany. The news that the German ambassador is changing is absolutely untrue. According to Foreign Minister Wang yesterday, Ambassador Jiang's return to China on leave is a routine recuperation. The government relies on him deeply and has no intention of changing him. He is expected to return to Europe to take office after the autumn cools down.
