After the French Radio Station Stopped Receiving Commercial Telegrams 157

The Wusong Shanghai Coastal Radio Station Suddenly Became Busy

The Gushajiazhai radio station in the French Concession was privately established by the French, infringing on China's sovereignty. The government has negotiated for more than ten years. The International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications ordered the Wusong Shanghai Coastal Radio Station to do its best to rectify and improve. The person in charge of the Wusong Shanghai Radio Station supervised the station staff to send all incoming telegrams from ships by telephone first to avoid excuses for foreigners. The French Embassy agreed to inform the French station to stop receiving commercial telegrams from the 15th of this month. Now, various companies and foreign firms in this city use the Wusong Shanghai Coastal Radio Station for quick transmission and efficient service, and they are very satisfied and trust it very much. Therefore, the station's business has increased sharply recently and it is overwhelmed.

Yongpu Steamer Robbed in Shipu Waters 158

Disguised as Military Police, Harbor Police Disarmed

Over Ten Passengers Kidnapped, Losses Exceed Ten Thousand

Pirates are rampant in the coastal areas of Zhejiang, frequently robbing merchant ships. This time, the Yongpu steamer traveling to Shipu was again attacked by pirates, and over ten passengers were kidnapped. Yesterday, a gentleman came to Shanghai from Shipu. The reporter met him on the way and inquired about the truth of the robbery. He provided a detailed account, which is recorded below:

Pirates Boarded the Ship. Shipu, located south of Sanmen Bay, is an important coastal area under the jurisdiction of Xiangshan County, lined with shops. Since the Shanghai-Taiwan liner began operating, commerce in the area has flourished even more. Shanghai steamers arrive at the port daily, but for those inner harbors that Shanghai steamers cannot reach, smaller vessels like the Yongpu and Haiyou operate to Sizhou, Ninghai, Yuejin, and other ports, connecting with the Shanghai-Taiwan liners. On the 19th of this month, when the Yongpu steamer departed from Shipu, over thirty pirates disguised as military police, mostly wearing old and torn uniforms, boarded the ship. The crew did not suspect anything. However, as soon as the ship left the Shipu sea area, they launched their robbery.

Details of the Robbery. When the Yongpu steamer arrived at the waters of the Xunjiansi area, one of the pirates came out of the cabin and shouted. The pirates then took out their pistols, first disarming the four harbor police escorting the ship and locking them in the lower cabin. They then went to the wheelhouse, monitored the captain, and drove the crew into a room. The pirates then opened the purser's office and searched for cash, then robbed each passenger on board, one by one, taking all their silver, jewelry, clothing, and other items, totaling a loss of 15,000 to 16,000 yuan. The stolen goods were piled up in one place and guarded by the pirates.

Kidnapping of Passengers. The pirates forced the shipowner to sail east, lasting for a day and a night. When the ship arrived at the waters of Haimen, the pirates' robbery goals had been achieved. They then frantically blew the ship's whistle, and a pirate ship immediately arrived in response, as if it had been prearranged. Approaching the Yongpu steamer, they moved all the stolen goods onto the pirate ship. Before leaving, they kidnapped over ten passengers on board, mostly businessmen. The pirates also wanted to dismantle the ship's engine parts, but the captain repeatedly begged, and they were spared.

Report on Return to Port. The steamer was robbed by pirates for four days and four nights. The company was anxious day and night and unable to know its whereabouts. On the 24th, the Yongpu steamer was finally released by the pirates and returned to Shipu, but when it arrived at the port, the crew and passengers were all empty-handed, having lost all their money and belongings. The families of those kidnapped wept inconsolably upon hearing the news. The captain reported the details of the pirate attack to the company to request the offshore police department to pursue the pirates.

Aftermath. After the Yongpu returned to Shipu, the company telegraphed the Shanghai Naval Headquarters, requesting them to quickly send warships to pursue the pirates. After the Yongpu robbery, the Shanghai-Taiwan liners in the port proposed preventive measures, paying close attention to passengers boarding the ships. Anyone with suspicious behavior or unclear addresses would be refused boarding to avoid major dangers.

Shanghai Factories Again Request Postponement of the Factory Law 159

The Factory Law was promulgated by the National Government last year and was scheduled to take effect on February 1st of this year. However, due to requests from factories in various provinces to postpone the implementation, the Ministry of Industry, considering all parties, specially obtained approval from the National Government to postpone it for six months, setting the implementation date to August 1st. It is now learned that the Shanghai factories, as the implementation date of the Factory Law approaches, and due to the recent unrest in the country, will soon submit a request to the Ministry of Industry to postpone it again for six months to allow for careful discussion.

Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau Established on July 1st 160

The Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau has moved to the Liu Hongji Building and will be officially established on July 1st. Yesterday, the bureau sent letters to various agencies in the port for their information and notification. The original text is recorded below:

Official Letter:

We hereby inform you that we have received Order No. 121 from the Ministry of Communications, appointing Xi Dingmo as the acting director of the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau. We have also received Order No. 2009 from the Ministry of Communications, issuing a copper seal engraved with "Director of the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, Ministry of Communications," etc. In accordance with this, we have been legally organized, designated the building at No. 6 Sichuan Road in the Public Concession as the bureau's address, and will be officially established on July 1st. In addition to submitting reports separately and sending letters, we hereby inform you for your reference.

Notice:

This bureau is ordered by the Ministry of Communications of the National Government to handle maritime affairs. All matters concerning the registration, inspection, measurement, load lines, markings, seamen, navigation routes, shipbuilding, issuance of licenses, and verification of entry and exit of ships navigating within the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui shall be under the jurisdiction of this bureau. In accordance with legal organization, we will be officially established on July 1st. The bureau's address is located at No. 6 Sichuan Road in the Public Concession. Please take note of this notice.

Shanghai Municipal Government Municipal Meeting 166

183rd Meeting

The Municipal Government held its 183rd municipal meeting on June 19, 20. Those present were Yu Hongjun, Sun Baorong, Zhou Liangcai, Cai Zengji, Zhu Yan, Pan Gongzhan, Shen Yi, Chen Xizeng, Hu Hongji, Xu Peihuang, and Huang Boqiao. The chairman was the mayor, and the record was taken by (Xiang Yu'en, on behalf). (A) Matters for reporting: 1. Secretary-General's report: (1) The case of the reorganization of the city in accordance with the City Organization Law has been handled by the government's order to various bureaus. Regarding the position of secretary in each bureau, the four bureaus of political society, public security, and public utility have reported and submitted them for review. (2) All bureaus must request approval for hiring and entrusting specialized personnel or establishing affiliated institutions. Hope all bureaus pay attention. 2. The directors and counselors of each bureau have separate mimeographed reports. (B) Matters for discussion: (1) The matter of cleaning the roads is planned to be taken over by the Health Bureau from July 1st. The resolution was passed. (2) It is proposed to formulate rules for the disposal of vehicles and ships with unpaid donations and the sale of objects for public use. The resolution, the original proposed rules are not suitable for implementation, and the Finance Bureau should submit another case to the government for review and handling. (3) The plan and chart of the small road system in the eastern part of the South Shanghai District. The resolution was passed as submitted. (4) The Social Bureau requested the collection of civilian land in the triangular field between Lao Ximen Fangxie Road and Zhonghua Road to build a National Goods Exhibition Hall and a National Goods Shopping Mall. The resolution was passed, one, through, but the construction estimate and other plans were decided by the Social Bureau in conjunction with the Finance, Land, and Public Works Bureaus. Two, the construction funds were the responsibility of the Social and Finance Bureaus, and they contacted the Municipal Chamber of Commerce or banks to raise funds. Three, the Ministry of Internal Affairs was consulted, and the Public Works and Land Bureaus were notified. (5) The resolution on determining the number of the second phase of public bonds to be issued was postponed. (6) Continued discussion on the matter of constructing buildings and acquiring land on both sides of roads built beyond the boundaries in this city. Can the matter be handled in accordance with the regulations on road construction fees? The resolution was passed in accordance with the review opinions (construction and land acquisition on both sides of roads built by the Bureau of Industry and Commerce beyond the boundaries should be handled in accordance with the regulations on road construction fees, but the project fee should be exempted before the roads are recovered). (7) Should Shanghai Bank's request to build its own wharf along the Wusong River along Maigen Road be approved? The resolution was approved for flexible handling given the special circumstances.

ICB Deadline to Demolish Shacks, Shack Dwellers' Earnest Appeal 170

Appeal to Taxpaying Chinese Association

Hoping to Use Foreign Staff's Salaries to Build Houses

Zhu Xueili, Cao Xukun, Xu Naikui, Liu Jinzhu, and other representatives of the shacks in Yangshupu protested to the ICB because the ICB set a deadline of July 1st to demolish all shacks. They also sent a letter to the Shanghai Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association, requesting assistance. The letter said: We hereby inform you that the representatives have been renting land in the Yangshupu area for a long time and have built shacks to shelter themselves from the wind and rain. Although life is difficult, we have not violated any criminal laws. Although the occupation is humble, it should be protected by law. However, the ICB sent police to notify us that more than 1,000 shacks must be demolished by July 1st, which is tyrannical and cruel and will put more than 1,000 households of old and young to death. The ICB's intention is nothing more than to consider public security, hygiene, and fire safety, thinking that the place where the shack dwellers live is the source of all evil. They do not hesitate to despise humanity and destroy the law to carry out this nest-destroying act. It has been found that riots and violations, as well as hiding dirt and filth, mostly occur in prosperous areas of the city, and the lairs of thieves and kidnappers are also mostly in the city. According to statistics, this is credible. If it is recognized that there are violations and the cracking of thieves in the shack area, it must be demolished, then the first to be demolished should be the city, not the shacks. If the ICB has already demolished the houses in the city, the shack dwellers will have to endure it. Otherwise, they will swear to resist the illegal infringement to the death. In terms of hygiene, it is even more tragic. Although the shack dwellers have no real estate and do not pay direct taxes, the transfer of indirect taxes has increased without limit. The shack dwellers have no power to resist and bear the burden of death. How much does the ICB collect in total municipal donations each year and how many miscellaneous donations? May I ask if even one ten-millionth of it has been used for hygiene equipment in the shack area? Has the ICB ever had hygiene facilities that were opposed or destroyed by the shack dwellers? The laborers of the shack dwellers barely earn enough to eat and clothe themselves, so how can they have the surplus to engage in hygiene equipment? The ICB does not blame itself for its dereliction of duty, but instead thinks that the shacks are guilty. What is more unfair in the world than this? As for the fire problem, if it is proved by statistics, the city is more, and the shacks are less. The truth is that the lives and property of the shack dwellers are located there, and they are always vigilant. It is not like the residents in the city who have fire insurance and can sit back and watch the fire, letting it spread, and then calmly collect compensation afterward. Moreover, the shacks are separated from the city, and even if there is a fire, it is difficult to suffer. The above three points, even if the blame lies with the shacks, the ICB has no reason to demolish them all except to find ways to improve them. Moreover, the shacks have no guilt at all, but they are still subjected to this cruel treatment. The ICB cannot be exempted from the responsibility of compensation for damages. Not only that, if once this more than 1,000 homeless shack dwellers are demolished by the deadline, they will be displaced, the old and weak will be abandoned in the ditches, and the strong will take risks. This is the inevitable trend. Moreover, if this more than 1,000 shacks think that people's property should be protected by law, Article 17 of the Provisional Constitution has clear provisions, and according to criminal law, it can also be properly defended against illegal infringement. May I ask if the ICB also regards it as a thug and shoots it with machine guns? If a change is brewed, can the ICB be exempted from responsibility? Even more, the Shanghai Municipal Government has built hundreds of bungalows for the shack dwellers and ordered them to move in because the shacks are not hygienic. The city's annual income is more than doubled compared with the ICB. It can still find a place to live for the poor. The ICB wastes huge sums of money every year and seeks the pleasure of family members for foreign employees in every possible way. Alas, our shacks not only cannot get a little bit of it, but even the original home is arbitrarily destroyed. If the ICB has a little humanity, it only needs to move the annual salary of one foreign employee to build hundreds of thousands of bungalows. The shack dwellers are willing to repay it in monthly installments after eating. Now, relying on the sharpness of guns and artillery, the shack dwellers are put to death. No wonder the radical redification is becoming more and more rampant. It is this generation who has forced and brewed it. The shack dwellers have been toiling for a long time and have been supplied with knives. Now, if they are more aggressive and if they submit again, then there will be no eggs under the cover. In addition to entrusting lawyer You Zhi to protect it according to law and protesting to the ICB, I am afraid that the ICB will rely on its violence and despise the law. I am here to cry before your meeting again. I beg you to show your compassion and reason with the ICB, so that thousands of old and weak households will not be displaced. Otherwise, when the violence comes, the shack dwellers have sworn to die. The May 30th Massacre will not be difficult to see again. It is not a dare to alarm people with dangerous words, but it is also true that they are forced to be here. I beg you to be considerate.

Ma Ruixiang's head injury is roughly the same as Qu's, but the knife mark is about an inch longer than Qu's. The molars cannot function when eating. Yin Wenlong's Family Accuses China National Aviation Corporation 173

The Lawsuit Was Filed in the Special District Court the Other Day

Requesting 50,000 Yuan in Compensation for Maintenance and Comfort

On December 9th of last year, when the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai No. 2 aircraft flew to Wuhan, it collided with the large mast of a sand boat parked on the river bank shortly after taking off, the wing broke and the mast broke, and the plane crashed on the sandy beach by the river. The pilot, Bell, the assistant, Bian Fugen, the passenger, the Russian woman Edith Wen, and the bodyguard of Commander Xiong, Zeng Chunfan, were seriously injured. Yang Yongchun, a military officer of the National Government, and Xiong Shihui, the commander of the Songhu Garrison, were also seriously injured. Yin Wenlong, a native of Wu County, the Chinese manager of the automobile department of Anli Yanghang in Hankou, whose wife Sun Yuefang had just given birth to a son on the 7th and was extremely happy, planned to return to Hankou to comfort her, also boarded the plane and died tragically from serious injuries. The details at the time were reported earlier. It is now learned that after the tragic death of Yin's brother Wenlin, he hired lawyer Tong Yuwen to send a letter to the company on the 13th of the same month, requesting compensation. The company's legal counsel, lawyers Li Zuyu and Shi Lin, firmly refused on the 17th based on the example of force majeure. Yin's brother then hired lawyer Liu Shifang and sent another letter to Li Shi on January 17th of this year to negotiate everything. Lawyer Li sent a letter on the 21st to firmly refuse. Yin then proceeded with litigation procedures on the one hand, and Tong and Liu made a warning letter on the other, limiting the time to give a satisfactory reply within three days, otherwise they would decide to file a lawsuit. The Chinese person in charge of the company was very willing to settle the matter quickly, but the American did not agree. The lawyer Liu Shifang and Tong Yuwen filed a lawsuit against China National Aviation Corporation on behalf of Yin Zibenrong, who was less than a month old, and his legal representative, Yin's wife Sun Yuefang, requesting compensation for: (1) funeral expenses, (2) maintenance expenses for the two plaintiffs, and (3) comfort money for the two plaintiffs, totaling 50,000 yuan, and bearing all litigation costs in the case. The lawsuit was filed in the Special District Court the other day (26th).

Silk Factory Wage Negotiations Break Down 175

Social Affairs Bureau to Mediate

A total of 106 silk factories in the city, including Tongyi, employing 45,000 female workers, 24,000 child laborers, and 4,200 male workers, considering the factories' operating losses and to show labor-management cooperation, agreed in October of last year to temporarily calculate wages at 85% of the original rate. The work schedule was changed to two shifts per month, and Sunday holidays were temporarily suspended until the end of May 1931, when everything would revert to the original terms. Now that the deadline has passed and the issuance of silk industry public bonds is imminent, the workers demanded a return to the previous conditions. However, the factories, citing poor market conditions, repeatedly delayed and refused to restore the original terms. The Silk Reeling Industry Association repeatedly sent representatives to negotiate with the Silk Industry Guild. As a result, the employers agreed to increase female workers' wages from 51 cents to 57 cents and to restore the work schedule to its original state of four days per month. Sunday holidays would pay female workers 20 cents, and child laborers 10 cents. The labor side immediately convened a meeting of representatives of all workers in the city to discuss solutions. However, the workers unanimously insisted that all wages, work schedules, holiday bonuses, and other benefits must be fully restored without any reduction, and they would not stop until their demands were met. Because the attitude of all the workers was so firm and to avoid any further unfortunate incidents, the union yesterday submitted a request to the Social Affairs Bureau, asking them to promptly convene a meeting of labor and management for mediation.

Cai Yuanpei Swindled Out of Fifty Dollars 180

Bold Swindlers Impersonate to Deceive

Many Households Have Been Deceived

Fortunately Discovered by Tang Haian

Four Swindlers Sentenced to Two Years Each

Several days ago, four uninvited guests suddenly visited the Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office. Some were dressed in Western suits, others in Zhongshan suits. They presented calling cards and requested an audience with Superintendent Tang Haian. Superintendent Tang, seeing the names "Liu Jucen, Qi Ziwen, Lin Ziqing, and Xu Shicai" on the cards, realized he did not know any of them. However, their intentions seemed quite serious, so he agreed to meet them. During the meeting, the four men claimed to be representatives from the Anhui Epidemic Hospital, sent to Shanghai to raise funds. They presented a donation book and asked Superintendent Tang to generously donate to support their good cause. After reviewing the donation book and questioning them in detail, Tang noticed many suspicious points. He suspected they were imposters trying to swindle money. He immediately detained them and telephoned the Xinzha Police Station, who sent detectives to arrest the four men and seize the donation book. They also went to Liu's residence at 733 Edward Road and found a large box of forged seals and several donation books. The four were immediately imprisoned, and an investigation was launched. It has now been determined that many households in the city have been deceived. Notable victims include the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Securities and Commodities Exchange. However, the fraudulent schemes were not uniform. When defrauding the Banks of China and Communications, they used the name of the National Tour and Inspection Group. Each bank was swindled out of ten dollars, or sometimes four or five dollars. The Chinese Cotton Mill Association on Edward Road was swindled out of forty dollars, under the guise of establishing an industrial factory to support wounded soldiers from the 1911 Revolution. They even used this pretext to swindle fifty dollars from Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica. The audacity of their actions is evident. Yesterday morning, the police brought the representatives of the deceived businesses, along with Liu and the others, to the Special District Court for investigation. Judge Wu Tingqi questioned them. The four defendants, Liu and the others, confessed that they had been driven by economic hardship to commit fraud. Judge Wu reviewed the confessions and sentenced Liu, Qi, Lin, and Xu to two years of imprisonment each for habitual fraud. The donation books and seals were confiscated.

Inside Story of the Suicide Pact is Tragic 181

Female Protagonist Saved,

But May Be Rejected By Husband

Tears of Regret in Court

Kindness of Police Lawyer

Zhang Panqin, a foreman from Pudong working at the Zhonghua Industrial Company in Caojiadu, had an affair with Yao Gu, a woman living in the same building. Annoyed by his wife Zhang Ji's nagging, Zhang Panqin contemplated suicide. He and Gu went to Room 318 of the Andong Hotel on Hubei Road and ingested opium. Zhang soon died from poisoning, and his body has been reported to the authorities and confirmed. It was ordered to be collected and buried. Gu was sent to the hospital for treatment. This information has been reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that Gu's husband, Yao, is from Changzhou and works as a general affairs clerk at a school in the French Concession.

Room and board are provided at the school, and he only returns home once a week. Gu, although 32 years old, is not accustomed to living alone, which is why she became acquainted with Zhang, leading to this tragic love suicide. After Gu recovered, the police believed that, even though it was suicide, she should be held legally responsible. They brought her before the Summary Court of the Special District Court. The judge believed that she had

suspicion of inciting suicide and ordered that she be prosecuted in the local court. Yesterday morning, the police representative, lawyer Ru Baoyi, filed a lawsuit against Gu based on Article 290 of the Criminal Law. Presiding Judge Zhou Han opened the court and questioned her. Lawyer Ru stated the case and said that, according to the third clause of the law, those who plan to die together may be exempted from punishment. He asked the court to consider whether the defendant was eligible for this clause. When questioned, Yao Gu stated that she originally lived at 71 Renshou Lane, Bailinan Road. Zhang Panqin and his wife also lived in the same building. Three months ago, Zhang's wife, Ji, returned to her hometown to give birth, leaving Zhang alone. At this time,

an affair developed between us. Later, due to gossip, I moved to a room in 95 Xinkang Lane, Bailinan Road. Unexpectedly, Zhang could not forget me and moved his family to the upper floor of the same building. Since then, I have been constantly subjected to his wife Ji's jealousy. On the 21st of this month, the couple argued again because of this. To avoid further trouble, I went out the next day and took a streetcar to Nanjing Road, intending to transfer to the Route 5 streetcar and go to the French Concession to discuss moving with my husband. Unexpectedly, Zhang

waited for me at the streetcar station. I was forced to go with him to the Andong Hotel to commit suicide together. I have a son and a daughter; how could I bear to leave them? Seeing that I was unwilling to be a lovebird to the death, Zhang threatened to strangle me with a rope. I had no choice but to follow him. Zhang then took out opium paste, rolled it into a ball, and I swallowed ten pills. He only took four or five pills. Zhang had prepared the suicide note at home in advance. After arriving at the hotel, I wrote a letter to my mother, stating the reasons for this suicide. Zhang also said at the time that we

were committing suicide because of love and that the reports in the newspapers would bring great fame. My brothers and uncles all work at the Tongshang Trust Company, so I really did not want to die. I only complied because I was coerced. Now, if my husband is still willing to forgive me for my flaws and take me back, I swear to turn over a new leaf and abide by the virtues of a woman to make up for my past mistakes. If there is no hope of reconciliation, I will only throw myself into the Jiliang Institute. At this point, she seemed very distressed, and tears flowed down her face. The police lawyer immediately stated that, according to this situation, Gu may not have incited suicide. According to her testimony, she ingested more opium than the deceased. However, her husband has

disowned her since this case. Her husband was not present in court today, which proves this. Therefore, if the case is ruled in her favor, it will be difficult for her to find a place to live and this could drive her to attempt suicide again. If she is sent to the Jiliang Institute, as she requested, her children would be left without anyone to care for them. For the sake of both parties, the presiding judge should summon her husband, Yao, to court and persuade him. Yao may recall their past affection and restore their old relationship, so that the couple can be reunited. Presiding Judge Zhou deeply believed that the lawyer's statement was insightful and ruled Yao Gu innocent, but she will be temporarily held at the detention center while awaiting the summons of her husband for further review.

Yangtse to Offer Pootoo Service 182

Butterfield & Swire Assigns the New Peking

Foreign Ships Directly Enter Our Inland Waterways

Motive for Opening the Route: Every summer, Chinese shipping companies such as China Merchants, Sanbei, and Ping'an often offer the Pootoo service to facilitate passengers seeking refuge from the heat. Pootoo has excellent scenery, and it only takes a few hours to reach from Ningbo. Most Chinese shipping lines in this port use ships from the Shanghai-Ningbo and Shanghai-Taiwan routes, adding a Pootoo stop on their weekly schedules. Now, as the ships are beginning their service, the number of Westerners in Shanghai seeking refuge there is increasing daily. Therefore, they specifically requested that the British-owned Butterfield & Swire company also offer a Pootoo route for Western passengers. Butterfield & Swire has agreed and will begin operating the route with ships from July onwards.

Assigned Schedule: Butterfield & Swire has decided to use the New Peking, a ship on the Shanghai-Ningbo route, to inaugurate the Pootoo service. Every Friday, the ship will depart from Shanghai, first arrive at Ningbo, and then proceed to Pootoo. The first trip is scheduled for July 3rd, and eight trips are planned. While the business is mainly aimed at Westerners, Chinese passengers will still be carried.

Business Situation: Butterfield & Swire's operation of the Pootoo route is a pioneering venture. The company has decided that each departure will reserve thirty seats in the main dining room specifically for Western passengers, while the remaining seats will be available for Chinese passengers. Each Western passenger seat is priced at 1,500 yuan, and the eight trips will generate 12,000 yuan in revenue. This is the first time a foreign ship has operated in Pootoo, and it seems to infringe on China's maritime rights.

Girl Not Yet Sixteen Years Old

Assassination Case in Xujiahui 185

Six Knife Wounds, Intestines Spilled Out

Murder Weapon Still Lodged in Neck

Yesterday, an unidentified male corpse was discovered in the Zhangjiabang area behind the Hujiazhai residence, west of Xujiahui town. The villagers reported it to the Second Precinct of the Sixth District. Upon receiving the report, Chief Liu led the police to investigate. The corpse was a man in his thirties, wearing a blue cloth shirt and trousers, yellow socks, and cloth shoes. He was lying on the bank of the river, head to the east and feet to the west. He had six knife wounds on his body, and his intestines were spilling out, a gruesome sight. An eight-inch-long sharp knife was still lodged in his neck, not removed. However, there was no blood on the ground. The area was very remote. It is presumed that he was murdered elsewhere and the body was moved to this location. It was very close to Hongqiao Road, only about a hundred steps away. He ordered the local Baojia, Wang Maogong, to report to the court for an autopsy. At 4:00 pm yesterday, prosecutor Zhao Zhiji was commissioned to arrive at the scene for the autopsy. The autopsy confirmed that the corpse was indeed murdered. As no family members were found, he ordered the Baojia to prepare a coffin for burial and to send the knife to be kept on file, pending investigation of the murderer.

The lake bandits Xue Wu, Xue Guoqing, and Yang Yinshan were sentenced to death for robbing a stone boat on Dian Shan Lake. Because the crimes of the bandits were extremely heinous, they were all sentenced to death. Xue Guoqing replied from Funing, residing in Yangshupu, and requested to write a letter to Xue Guoxian, notifying his parents. Bizarre Goose Case 187

All People on the Boat Have Disappeared

Limited Number of Geese Remaining

West of Kunshan Station along the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, about three miles north of Zhengyi Station in the countryside of Jiangqiao, a large number of white geese, about a thousand, were discovered on the morning of the 24th of this month, eating rice seedlings in the fields. When the local villagers saw them, they thought they were swans and gathered to catch them, killing dozens of them. The villagers took them home to cook. Around 4:00 pm, the Zhengyi branch of the Kunshan County Public Security Bureau found out and sent police officers to investigate. The officers returned to the bureau and reported that there were a total of 973 white geese. A chicken and duck shop in Fengmen, Suzhou, hired two boats to transport the geese to Shipai Town on the border of Kunshan and Bacheng for sale. There was a shop owner, three crew members, and a child on the boats. They sailed along the Suzhou Pond and passed through Zhengyi Harbor from south to north on the afternoon of the 23rd. In the evening, they stopped for the night at Jujiang Bridge, about three miles from the town. For unknown reasons, all the people on the boats disappeared, leaving only an empty boat. It is said that only about two hundred or so white geese remain. The whereabouts of the boatmen are unknown. The local Public Security Area is currently sending police officers to investigate the truth of this case in detail for further action.

Summer Calibration of Measures 188

The measures used by the Shanghai rice industry must be obtained from Rengutang and can only be used after calibration. Rengutang has a fixed rule of calibrating measures four times a year, in spring, summer, autumn, and winter. This summer's calibration was scheduled for the two days before yesterday and was held in the main hall of the Cuixiu Hall in the City Temple. For this calibration, the leaders selected twenty experienced measurers after discussion and invited rice industry groups to supervise the process. Each measure was first inspected by the leaders before it could be calibrated. The Rengu, Nanbang, and Beibang San Gonghui then affixed calibration lists and branded them with hot irons to ensure meticulousness. It is said that more than nine hundred measures were calibrated during the two days.

Jianghai Customs Changes Tax Rates for Kerosene, etc. 189

Loford, the Commissioner of Customs for Jianghai Customs, has made separate changes to the tax rates for imported gasoline and kerosene. He issued a special notice yesterday, stating that the tax rates for all imported gasoline, kerosene, etc., will be changed separately starting from July 1, 1931, for the information of all merchants. The changes are as follows: Tariff Number 482 for imported mineral gasoline, naphtha, and benzine: A. Cased, 1.63 Customs Gold Units per 10-gallon case; B. Bulk, 1.53 Customs Gold Units per 10 gallons. Tariff Number 495 for imported kerosene: A. Cased, 1.43 Customs Gold Units per 10-gallon case; B. Bulk, 1.33 Customs Gold Units per 10 gallons.

A Heinous Family Tragedy: Seeking Re-examination to Avenge a Sister 190

Yueying, the 22-year-old daughter of farmer He Lingen from Hejiatang, Twenty-sixth Ward, Southwest Township, Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Road, married Yonggen, the son of farmer Zhu Guanbao from No. 3, Zhujiazhai, nearby, through a matchmaker last spring, April. After the marriage, the couple's relationship was considered harmonious. However, the husband's aunt, Zhang, who was over fifty years old, still possessed a flirtatious nature, resulting in a widespread notorious reputation, known to everyone in the vicinity. She was also extremely fierce. Furthermore, Yonggen was also having an affair with a woman surnamed Mou from a neighboring family. As a result, the husband and his parents treated Yueying almost like a thorn in their side, frequently abusing her, even to the point of beating her. The atmosphere within the family was like hell. Unable to bear it, she returned to her mother's home to weep and complain. After her father, Wu Lingen, kindly consoled her, he sent her back to the Zhu family multiple times. On the twelfth of this month, Yueying, again due to a minor quarrel, returned to her mother's home to stay temporarily. On the day before yesterday (the 25th), at 4 p.m., Yueying returned home alone. When she left, her expression was cheerful, and there was nothing unusual about her. However, at around 9 p.m. that evening, Yueying suddenly hanged herself in her room. After someone reported this to her father, Wu Lingen, he rushed to investigate and found wounds on Yueying's body. Consequently, he reported this to the Sixth District Third Sub-precinct, requesting an investigation and arrest. After receiving the report, Chief Liu immediately dispatched Officer Yuan and police officers to the scene. Zhu Guanbao and his son had already fled. Only Zhang was at home. Examining the body, they found a purplish-red mark around the neck, several red wounds on the right side and left armpit, and faint bluish-red bruises visible on the outside of the right knee. It was confirmed that she had hanged herself after being beaten to death. Upon investigating the neighbors, it was confirmed that they had heard cries for help that evening. Therefore, Zhu Zhang was taken to the precinct for further investigation. Chief Liu also instructed Zhao Hongxiang, the local ward head, to report the matter to the court for an inquest. Prosecutor Wu was commissioned to conduct an inquest in the countryside. The inquest determined that the deceased had indeed died by hanging herself before death. The family was instructed to prepare a coffin for burial. However, the deceased's elder sister, Wu Xiqing (a current teacher), believed that her sister's death was suspicious. Yesterday, she submitted a written request to the court for a re-examination. Simultaneously, she reported to the precinct, requesting that they find a way to arrest Zhu Guanbao and Zhu Yonggen, father and son. After a preliminary hearing by the precinct chief, Wu Lingen, the deceased's father, recounted the previous events and pleaded for justice on her behalf. According to Zhu Zhang's statement, she was 52 years old. Her daughter-in-law, Wu, returned home at 4 p.m. yesterday. Because her husband was working at the China Cemetery, and she and her son were working in the fields, neither of them was at home. After returning home, Wu asked her for the key, opened the door, and went back out to work. When she returned home in the evening, Zhang cooked, and the daughter-in-law fetched water by the riverside, returned to her room to do laundry, and closed the door. When her son, Yonggen, returned to the room, he asked her to eat dinner. Unexpectedly, Wu had already hanged herself from the horizontal beam in front of the bed. Yonggen immediately rushed forward to take her down, but she had already died. Zhu Guanbao and his son gave statements that were largely the same as Zhang's. However, they vehemently denied any beating or abuse. Chief Liu, considering that the case involved a life, sent Zhu Guanbao, Zhu Yonggen, Zhu Zhang, along with Wu Lingen, the deceased's father, to the bureau for review.

The "Consumption Inevitably Leads to Death" Theory and New Treatments for Lung Disease 192

Copied and translated from a German journal on tuberculosis.

(1) The Origin of the "Consumption Inevitably Leads to Death" Theory

Xingzhi　　　often. But the difficulty for doctors.　Spreads widely. There is nothing quite like tuberculosis (i.e., consumption). Tuberculosis attacks us.　　　　. Without interruption. It is the most harmful and deadly infectious disease. It is what we fear the most. Since ancient times, it has been determined to be 　　　　 a certain death　. Because it is truly difficult to treat after contracting it. Therefore, doctors are at a loss when they encounter it. Patients who contract it are filled with fear and despair. Every day, there is the worry of　　　　　. But in modern times. With the advancement of medicine and the emergence of famous doctors, precise research has shown that tuberculosis is not necessarily an incurable disease. If 　　　　 method　 is used. Eight or nine out of ten who are treated in the early stages are cured. Even those in the second or third stage have hope of recovery.　 If the disease has been contracted for too long. After　　　　, patients in the terminal stage have no way to be saved. However, contracting a disease for so long that it cannot be treated is not unique to tuberculosis. It is hoped that those who contract this disease will not neglect treatment in the early and middle stages. Treatment and recuperation is possible.

(2) The Discovery of the Tuberculosis Pathogen

Since ancient times, the medical communities of both the East and the West have had many empty theories and conjectures about the cause of tuberculosis. All were dark and unclear. Recently, the German　　　　 scholar Dr. Koch discovered that the tuberculosis bacterium is the cause of tuberculosis. This broke through thousands of years of darkness and shone a ray of great light. Just as the cholera bacterium is the cause of cholera, the diphtheria bacterium is the cause of diphtheria, and the dysentery bacterium is the cause of dysentery. Other diseases, such as syphilis, are caused by the syphilis spirochete, and leprosy is caused by the leprosy bacillus. This is known throughout the world. Tuberculosis is also the same. The cause of its occurrence is the tuberculosis bacillus. This bacillus most likes to attack humans. It mainly lives and breeds in our lungs. The number of humans harmed by it is countless. In the past, it accounted for one-seventh of the world's population. In modern times, it accounts for one-sixth. In cities, it reaches one-fifth. It is truly the most widespread infectious disease.

(3) The Two Great Benefactors of Those with Lung Disease

(1) Dr. Robert Koch of Germany. He was born in 1843 in the city of Klausthal, Germany. His family was quite well-off. Therefore, he was able to focus on his studies from a young age. After graduating from middle school, he attended various universities in the country to study medicine. Before the age of thirty, he discovered the bacteria responsible for　. Famous doctors in the country were captivated by his work. Several years later, on March 24, 1882, Dr. Koch presented his research on the tuberculosis bacillus at the German Physiological Society in Berlin. At the time, the medical communities of various countries were shaken by it. The German government praised his scholarship and appointed Dr. Koch as the director of the Institute of Hygiene. Emperors from various countries also presented him with high-level medals. Universities from various countries competed to send him honorary degrees. In 1905, the Nobel Prize in Medicine was also awarded to the old doctor. He can be said to have achieved the highest honor in the academic world. Those who treat tuberculosis today all base their work on Koch's discovery. His contribution to saving lives and helping the world is something that humanity around the world should be grateful for.

(2) Dr. Bergell of Germany. Since Dr. Koch discovered the tuberculosis bacillus as the cause of tuberculosis, scholars of tuberculosis in the East and the West have competed to conduct research, hoping to find a miraculous way to kill this bacillus. However, the results have all been failures. This is because ordinary doctors in the past did not understand that the tuberculosis bacillus has a unique and special structure. After Dr. Bergell's painstaking research, he discovered that the tuberculosis bacillus has a special defense that can resist all external medicinal attacks. The tuberculosis bacillus is composed of an inner membrane of neutral fat and an outer membrane of acid-fast wax.

If a method is not found to destroy the wax barrier and disarm the fatty armament, then there is no way to capture the tuberculosis bacillus and put it to death. Therefore, Dr. Bergell, the great benefactor of all lung disease sufferers in the world, collected all kinds of medicinal substances from animals, plants, and minerals, and conducted painstaking research for decades. It is unknown how much brainpower he exhausted and how many times his heart membrane gland compressed his juice. There is a special effective component that has a strong dewaxing effect on the tuberculosis bacillus. This is truly a great success in the fundamental treatment of tuberculosis, a question that has never been answered in thousands of years of medical history.

German Dr. Natterer's Map of the Distribution of Pulmonary Arteries and Bronchial Tubes

(4) Special Efficacy Treatment of Pulmonary Tuberculosis

Pulmonary tuberculosis (i.e. consumption) is caused by the tuberculosis bacillus. When this bacillus enters the human body, it forms nodules in that area to cut off the flow of blood. The tuberculosis bacillus can also secrete an acid-fast wax to surround its body, preventing the invasion of all external medicinal powers, so even if various bactericidal drugs are used, either internally or by injection, they cannot reach the actual substance of the pathogen. The natural therapy, symptomatic therapy, physical therapy, serum therapy, pharmaceutical therapy, and other treatments that have been commonly used by doctors in the past have not been completely successful, and the saying that there is no cure for consumption has spread throughout the world. This is because they did not know this profound science. Therefore, modern tuberculosis scholars, based on the above-mentioned science, continue to research and spare no effort. The result is this chemical saint, named Sanosin, that kills all pulmonary tuberculosis bacilli. This medicine was invented and successfully developed according to the latest medical theory of German Dr. Koch, the inventor of the tuberculosis bacillus, and German Dr. Bergell, the inventor of the tuberculosis bacillus dewaxing technique. According to current experimental reports from tuberculosis sanatoriums in Germany, Switzerland, and other countries, this drug has the effect of penetrating the nodules and dissolving the wax of lung diseases, and has bactericidal power, which can radically cure pulmonary tuberculosis in stages one, two and three, and indeed has the special effect of omnipotence. In China, it has been tested by the Central Health Experiment Institute of the National Government, the medicinal properties are peaceful and non-toxic, and there are absolutely no side effects. A brief summary of the medical effects is as follows:

(1) If the medicinal power of "Sanosin" is tested in a test tube, after one minute, all tuberculosis bacilli disappear their acid resistance, and after three minutes, the pulmonary tuberculosis bacilli are completely killed, and none are spared.

(2) Animal experiments have found that "Sandixing" can penetrate into the tuberculosis nodules. An examination of the latent tuberculosis bacilli in the nodules shows that they have all lost their acid resistance. This is sufficient proof that the wax has completely dissolved.

(3) If patients take "Sanosin" internally for about a week, they will immediately see a good condition such as diluted phlegm and lowered body temperature.

(4) Continuing to take "Sanosin" internally for more than thirty to sixty days will show a visible increase in body weight, increased appetite, and all symptoms will gradually subside, eventually achieving the great achievement of returning to life.

Regulations on the Payment of Business Tax by the Grain Industry 195

The Shanghai Bean and Rice Merchants Association received a letter from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "We have received a letter from the Business Tax Preparation Office of the Shanghai Finance Bureau stating that your association stated in its official letter that the Shanghai bean and rice merchants have always paid the Brokerage Tax and do not need to pay the Business Tax again. However, the current Business Tax Regulations in this city list a grain industry, and the trade association is concerned and requests an explanation. We have sent a letter to inquire and reply so that we can forward it to you, etc. Approved. Upon investigation, the draft business tax rate table of this city, the grain industry item, refers specifically to those who sell grain. As for the merchants who act as agents for customers to buy and sell and have a brokerage license, they should be changed to business tax in accordance with Article 20 of the draft Business Tax Regulations of this city and collected at the old tax rate. The current tax rate is not included in the package. If we wait to die, it is not appropriate. For this reason, we tenants have no choice but to jointly express our difficulties in detail to your platform. I hope that your landlord will forgive me, understand the situation below, and approve the reduction of the rent of Taiyuan Lane by a certain percentage, to ease the burden and live a peaceful life, which is all given by your landlord, which is a great kindness, and there is no end to our gratitude, and we wait for your reply, how can we win the extreme expectation."

Elevator Suddenly Drops, Shaking One Person to Death 202

At 6:30 p.m. last night, at No. 3 Xinkang Road, Jiangxi Road, the upper-level elevator failed mechanically and suddenly dropped, causing a young man, about 20 years old and resembling a student, to be injured, damaging his vital parts. He was barely breathing. Later, the doorman there called police from Post 2158, who sent him to Renji Hospital in a car. The medical treatment was ineffective, and he soon died.

Chen Atang's Burial Place is Disturbed 203

Grave Site Sold Illegally by His Uncle

Chen Atang, a hawker who was brutally beaten to death by Japanese sailors five years ago, was seriously involved with the Japanese government after the tragic case, with the assistance of Wu Kaisheng, a lawyer, and the assistance of various groups. Negotiations were held and a lawsuit was filed with the Nagasaki District Court. As a result, two murderers were sentenced to two years of detention and two years of imprisonment, to be served concurrently for four years. The bereaved family of the deceased was given a consolation payment of 3,000 yuan to be used as follow-up alimony for the children and mother. A portion of it was used to purchase land near the Eighteen Hua Wharf in Pudong for his burial. The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau recently planned to purchase land in Pudong to establish a public cemetery. Chen Atang's uncle secretly sold the tomb without permission. The tomb will be destroyed soon. Chen Song, Atang's wife, was extremely sad and angry when she heard the news. She has been running around and crying out for days, appealing to the representatives of the various groups that provided assistance last time to provide remedies. Tong Lizhang, a member of the former Wu Kaisheng Lawyer's Office, agreed to send a letter to groups such as the French Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association, asking them to forward a letter to the Municipal Health Bureau, requesting that Chen Atang's tomb be preserved to retain diplomatic relics.

Lu Miaolang Drowned in Suzhou Creek 204

Lu Miaolang, a native of Lishui, was 19 years old. He was studying at the Yu Da Distillery in Gongyi Lane, Zhabei. He had completed his apprenticeship. However, he liked to swim. Because it was hot recently, he often went to the new garbage bridge every afternoon to jump into Suzhou Creek to show off his skills. At 3 p.m. the day before yesterday, he used the same trick again. Unexpectedly, a boat passed by, causing him to go under the boat, resulting in his drowning. It was not until night that the body was discovered. Yesterday, Shen Qishan, the ward head of the Tenth Ward, reported the matter to the Local Court for an autopsy.

Young Woman Sues to Recover Shared Property 205

Recently, the young woman Wang Qiuquan hired Jin Yu and Li Yuan, two lawyers, to represent her in filing a criminal lawsuit with the French Concession Public Concession against her brother Wang Ruixin and Zheng Yutian for colluding to embezzle the estate of her deceased father and requesting investigation, etc. The lawsuit is recorded as follows: For embezzling shared property, a private prosecution is filed according to law, requesting strict punishment. My deceased father, Wang Youtian, opened the Yongfengtai Southern Goods Store at the Dongxiaoqiao Caishi Street entrance under your jurisdiction. When starting the business, my uncle, Bosheng, and Dao invested 500 yuan. The second defendant, Zheng Yutian, did not invest, but for the sake of friendship, he obtained a dry stock share. Later, the shares under Bosheng's name were still merged by my deceased father's investment. Therefore, my deceased father held nine-tenths of the total share capital of the store, while the second defendant only held one-tenth. All business facilities and monetary income and expenditure were controlled by my deceased father independently, and the second defendant did not interfere. In addition, my deceased father also opened the Laoyuchang Southern Goods Store in Guanyintang, Lujia, under your jurisdiction, solely with his own funds and also managed it himself. As a result of the deceased father's efforts in operating the two stores, there was an annual surplus. For example, the assets of Yongfengtai alone were no less than 20,000 yuan, and the assets of Laoyuchang were also more than 8,000 yuan. However, after the deceased father passed away, there was a demand for the buildings of the Laoyuchang store, so the first defendant gave up the roof for 1,500 yuan. The store's topping price and working capital were all merged into Yongfengtai. Therefore, Yongfengtai accumulated nearly 30,000 yuan. My deceased father unfortunately passed away in January of this year, and all the property left behind was controlled by the first defendant. The complainant and the first defendant are siblings. Although the complainant is a woman, according to current laws, for all inheritances that began after the National Government took power, women, whether married or unmarried, have the right to inherit property, and the method of analysis has also been stipulated, and the number of children is equally divided. This situation is not only clearly defined by law, but also undisputed by the first defendant. It is expected that although the first defendant outwardly acknowledges the right of the complainant to inherit the deceased father's estate, he secretly destroys all untraceable movable property, such as deposits and goods, and debts owed to others. The complainant believed that the first defendant had such intentions, so she commissioned a lawyer to send a letter requesting an analysis. Unexpectedly, he was ridiculed by empty words. The first defendant colluded with the second defendant to publish a statement in the newspaper about the career that the deceased father had worked hard to create throughout his life, falsely claiming that the six shares under the deceased father's name had been merged with the second defendant and renamed Yongfengtai Yiji to continue operating. As for the descendants of the Wang family, there is no relationship. According to the original lawsuit report, Yongfengtai's capital was nine-tenths owned by the deceased father and is all fictional. How could the defendant be even more afraid that the complainant would sue in the location of the store? Later, he published a statement in the newspaper, falsely claiming that the store had been handed over clearly and had now returned to his home in Nanxiang to make the complainant feel difficult. The scheming of the defendants is extremely cunning. I respectfully check that regardless of the assets of Yongfengtai, the number of shares in the deceased father's name, it can be ignored. It is undeniable that it is the property shared by the defendants and the complainant. Now, the defendants published in the newspaper without legal procedures, falsely merging the claims, and without the permission of the co-owners. The signs of their actions have clearly violated Article 356, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. The second defendant's helping act should also be regarded as the principal offender in accordance with Article 42 of the Criminal Code. The complainant has filed a separate lawsuit requesting an incidental civil action. I request that the case be submitted for investigation, etc. Yesterday, when summoned for questioning, the defendant Wang Ruixin was represented by lawyer Zhu Shuzhen, and Zheng Yutian was represented by lawyer Zhou Xiaoan. Both unanimously objected to the plaintiff's claim that the jurisdiction was wrong. In addition, this case is a civil lawsuit in nature and should not be criminally accused. The official ordered him to leave and wait for a later date for continued questioning.

Two People Jump into the River 206

One Dead, One Alive

(1) Yesterday morning at 1:20 AM, an unidentified middle-aged man jumped into the Suzhou Creek from the Baidu Bridge. At the time, Water Patrol Officer No. 14 of the Customs was patrolling under the Zha Pu Road Bridge. He saw the man from afar and rushed to rescue him. Only a soft black-edged whip and a white straw hat were not sinking with him, so he caught them floating on the water surface. The officer immediately retrieved them and waited for a long time, but the man did not reappear. He then went to the Baidu Bridge to inquire with people cooling off, who claimed that the man who jumped into the river was wearing a black Indian silk long gown, was about thirty years old, but nothing else was known. The reason for his suicide was even more unclear. The officer, unable to get any useful information, took the dead man's hat back to the police station to wait for family members to identify it. (2) The day before yesterday at 5:40 PM, a middle-aged man jumped into the Suzhou Creek from the Zha Pu Road Bridge. At the time, detectives Ge Changsheng and Cheng Yongnian of the Customs Water Patrol were passing by on a motorboat on official business. Seeing this, they immediately tried to rescue the man, whose legs were paralyzed, making it difficult for him to move. The two detectives took him to the police station. He confessed that his name was Song Zhengda, 33 years old, from the Tangxi area of Hangzhou. He usually made a living as a peddler. Due to illness for many days, both legs became paralyzed and he could not walk, making it difficult to resume his old job. As a result, he had spent all his savings. He wanted to return home, but had no money for the journey, so he sought death. Upon hearing this, the detectives and other officers contributed a total of four dollars and forty cents in silver and eight cents in small coins, which were sent to the Dai Shenchang Steamship Company's Da'an small steamer at 2:00 PM yesterday to return him to his hometown.

Continental Trunk Factory Grand Opening Yesterday 208

The number of Western-style leather suitcases and trunks exported to Europe and the United States each year reaches two to three million. However, according to past achievements, there has been little progress. Tracing its origin, the manufacturing business is entirely entrusted to ignorant workers, who adhere to old methods and do not engage in research. This is why it has remained stagnant for so long. Now, Mr. Zhou Fuzhang, a merchant dealing in both Western medicine and leather goods, realizing this, and together with his younger brother and friends, established the Continental Leather Suitcase and Trunk Factory on East-West Huade Road. They hired top technicians, selected high-quality cowhide and raw materials, and supervised the manufacture of various sizes of leather suitcases, trunks, Western-style and joint boxes, camphor wood boxes, and travel-friendly light suitcases, all of which are readily available. Now, a general distribution center has been established at the intersection of Yingda Road and Xizang Road, and the grand opening was held on June 26 (yesterday), with a special discount for seven days.

Floating Corpse Washed Up on the Shore of Wusong 214

Yesterday morning, a floating corpse was washed up on the surface of the river at the Hanjian Wharf on Wusong Wai Ma Road. The corpse belonged to a male, about 20 years old, with a flat top hairstyle, wearing a moon white cloth shirt, dark blue cloth pants, a leather belt around his waist, and barefoot, resembling a boatman. After the discovery, the rescue bureau's patrol boat towed it to the rescue bureau's wharf, and the local Bao reported it to the local court. At 4:00 PM, prosecutor Zhao Ziji from Songjiang District came to Wusong to inspect the body. He found no wounds on the corpse and confirmed that he had drowned. He instructed the charitable hall to provide a coffin and burial, and to post notices for relatives to claim the body.

New-Style Laundry Industry: The New-Style Laundry Industry Trade Union held its 22nd Executive Committee meeting yesterday. (Other matters omitted.)

Local Yellow Wine Industry: The Local Yellow Wine Industry Trade Union held a general meeting at the Yuyuan Garden in the City God Temple yesterday regarding the government's takeover of the public sale in the 20th year of the Republic. Zheng Jiuyuan was elected chairman. The chairman reported that since the appointment of the director of the Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau, he had been soliciting bids everywhere. All tax collection offices in Shanghai were still contracted by merchants, who were required to pay a fixed amount and deposit money. This was nominally a government takeover, but in reality, it was still contracting. It was unanimously decided to jointly publish a denial with the sorghum liquor trade union. If the government did not implement the takeover, they would expose the inside story in the future and appeal to the higher authorities.

Weather Report 217

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky was cloudy and very hot, with thunderstorms. The weather in northern China and Shandong was overcast and rainy. There were southeast to southwest winds over the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. The air pressure in western China was decreasing. Furthermore, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 93.6 degrees and the lowest was 74.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 97.2 degrees and the lowest was 73.6 degrees.

Youth Garden

Pingying Summer Research Society 218

— Hong Lian

The members of the Pingying Society are all modern youths. Several genuine youths, living in this era, as long as your sensitivity has not been lost and your perception has not become numb, who would not feel a sense of youth's sorrow? The Pingying Society has this point. They publish "Pingying" every month, a small newspaper that reveals their genuine emotions. They cannot stand the ugliness of society and cannot bear the depression in their hearts. They express all the true emotions in their hearts that can be cursed.

Time is constantly advancing like flowing water, and the affairs of the Pingying Society are also advancing with the times. However, because the members of the organization are mostly middle school students, the society's finances are inevitably hit during the consumption period and they are constantly struggling in a difficult state. However, hot blood is boiling in their bodies. They are not discouraged by economic constraints, and they still hold the organization's purpose and move forward vigorously. Recently, there has been talk of establishing the Pingying Summer Research Society.

During last year's summer, they held the first summer research society, and the results were remarkable. People in Meilong all praised their great spirit and the encouraging potential of their school management skills. This year's summer will see the second summer research society, which is expected to surpass last year's. Currently, President Mei Hongying, Academic Director Mei Yonggeng, General Affairs Director Wang Linxu, and several others are preparing, and the preparations are largely complete. It has been decided that classes will begin on July 6th.

The purpose of the Pingying Summer Research Society is to use the summer vacation to conduct research in various academic fields, learn from each other, and strive for progress. It is divided into three levels: senior primary school first grade, second grade, and remedial classes. Each class has 40 to 50 students. The subjects are divided into four categories: Chinese, English, Arithmetic, and General Knowledge. The duration is five weeks. The society's address is still located at the Meilong Primary School in Meilong Town on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. The instructors are all members of the society.

The society holds a reading guidance weekly meeting every Saturday, where the president invites members to give weekly lectures in rotation, guiding reading methods, etc., and invites local celebrities to lecture on various topics to provide detailed guidance. Now, I wish them all the best in their efforts.
